# Remember childhood love
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8000
	desc = VIETmisc.8000.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_her_smile
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
	
	trigger = {
		#in_command = no
		NOT = { trait = celibate }
		NOT = { trait = homosexual }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = envious
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = lustful
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = depressed
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = hedonist
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = gregarious
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = proud
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Love
		name = VIETmisc.8000.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_remembering_childhood_love
			duration = 365
		}
	}
}

# Servant has crush on maid
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8001
	desc = VIETmisc.8001.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_her_smile
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = ambitious
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = wroth
		}			
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = proud
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Things will work out
		name = VIETmisc.8001.a
		piety = 1
	}	
	option = { # I am a grouchy cynical old person
		name = VIETmisc.8001.b
		random = {
			add_trait = cynical
			chance = 20
		}
		custom_tooltip = { text = VIETmisc.8001.b.tooltip } #nah I'm actually a tsundere lol lol lol
	}
	option = { # youth!
		name = VIETmisc.8001.c
		prestige = 1
	}
	option = { # People are scary!
		name = VIETmisc.8001.d
		trigger = {
			trait = shy
		}
		tooltip_info = shy
		random = {
			add_trait = paranoid
			chance = 5
		}
	}
}

# Character feels inspired
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8002
	desc = VIETmisc.8002.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_hyouka
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
	
	#trigger = {
	#	in_command = no
	#}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = ambitious
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = diligent
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = wroth
		}			
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = proud
		}			
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = depressed
		}			
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = stressed
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Things will work out
		name = VIETmisc.8002.a
		piety = 1
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = depressed
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = depressed
				chance = 20
			}
		}
	}
}

# Saw a mudcrab the other day
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8003

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
	
	trigger = {
		#in_command = no
		has_game_rule = {
			name = VIET_events_rules
			value = silly
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = craven
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = slothful
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = paranoid
		}			
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = gluttonous
		}
	}
	
	option = { # I've heard others say the same
		name = VIETmisc.8003.a
		prestige = -1
	}
}

# STOP YOU VIOLATED THE LAW
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8004
	desc = VIETmisc.8004.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_market
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
	
	trigger = {
		#in_command = no
		NOT = {
			has_game_rule = {
				name = VIET_events_rules
				value = serious
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
					
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.05
			has_character_flag = VIET_recruited_oblivion_guard
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = slothful
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = paranoid
		}			
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = arbitrary
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Good
		name = VIETmisc.8004.a
		prestige = 1
	}
	option = { # Reward the guard
		name = VIETmisc.8004.b
		wealth = -5
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_rewarded_oblivion_guard
			duration = 1000
		}
	}
	option = { # Recruit the guard!
		name = VIETmisc.8004.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_recruited_oblivion_guard }
			NOT = { trait = greedy }
			NOT = { trait = cruel }
			NOT = { trait = arbitrary }
			NOT = { trait = paranoid }
			NOT = { trait = proud }
		}
		set_character_flag = VIET_recruited_oblivion_guard 
		wealth = -10
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_rewarded_oblivion_guard
			duration = 1000
		}
		create_random_soldier = {
			random_traits = no
			dynasty = random
			religion = ROOT
			culture = ROOT
			female = no
			attributes = {
				martial = 10
			}
			health = 6
			trait = brave
			trait = zealous
			trait = just
			trait = kind
		}
		new_character = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_was_oblivion_guard
				duration = -1
			}
			prestige = 50
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_loyal_servant
				who = ROOT
				years = 100
			}
			random = {
				VIET_give_generic_weapon_effect = yes
				chance = 20
			}
		}
	}
}

# Courtier said something inappropriate
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8005
	desc = VIETmisc.8005.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		any_courtier = {
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			is_adult = yes
			in_command = no
			is_abroad = no
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = arbitrary
		}
	}
	
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				is_adult = yes
				in_command = no
				is_abroad = no
			}
			save_event_target_as = target_VIET_inappropriate_courtier
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Chastise
		name = VIETmisc.8005.a
		event_target:target_VIET_inappropriate_courtier = {
			prestige = -5
			opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_publically_chastised_me
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
			reverse_opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_inappropriate_speech
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Hinted subtly
		name = VIETmisc.8005.b
		event_target:target_VIET_inappropriate_courtier = {
			prestige = -2
			reverse_opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_inappropriate_speech
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Did not say anything
		name = VIETmisc.8005.c
		piety = -2
		random = {
			add_trait = content
			chance = 20
		}
		event_target:target_VIET_inappropriate_courtier = {
			prestige = -2
		}
	}
}

# Bridge in province collapsed
province_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8006
	desc = VIETmisc.8006.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_tuscan_country
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = VIET_province_bridge_collapse }
		owner = {
			is_nomadic = no
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 10000
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			NOT = { num_of_max_settlements = 5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			NOT = { num_of_max_settlements = 3 }
		}
	}
	

	option = { # Send in emergency resources
		name = VIETmisc.8006.a
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				stewardship = 8
			}
		}
		owner = {
			wealth = -40
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_helped_emergency_quickly
				duration = 1000
			}
			random_list = {
				70 = {}
				10 = { add_trait = charitable }
				10 = { add_trait = kind }
				10 = { add_trait = just }
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_bridge_fix_sooner }
		hidden_tooltip = {			
			random_list = {
				20 = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = VIET_province_bridge_collapse
						duration = 200
					}
				}
				30 = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = VIET_province_bridge_collapse
						duration = 400
					}
				}
				30 = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = VIET_province_bridge_collapse
						duration = 600
					}
				}
				20 = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = VIET_province_bridge_collapse
						duration = 800
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Reapers"
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = decrease_prosperity_custom_tooltip
				hidden_tooltip = {
					change_variable = { which = prosperity_value value = -2 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Send in some help
		name = VIETmisc.8006.b
		owner = {
			wealth = -15
		}
		custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_bridge_fix_okay }
		hidden_tooltip = {			
			random_list = {
				20 = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = VIET_province_bridge_collapse
						duration = 300
					}
				}
				30 = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = VIET_province_bridge_collapse
						duration = 600
					}
				}
				30 = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = VIET_province_bridge_collapse
						duration = 900
					}
				}
				20 = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = VIET_province_bridge_collapse
						duration = 1200
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Reapers"
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = decrease_prosperity_custom_tooltip
				hidden_tooltip = {
					change_variable = { which = prosperity_value value = -3 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Do nothing
		name = VIETmisc.8006.c
		owner = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_ignored_emergency
				duration = 1500
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_bridge_fix_bad }
		hidden_tooltip = {			
			random_list = {
				20 = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = VIET_province_bridge_collapse
						duration = 400
					}
				}
				30 = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = VIET_province_bridge_collapse
						duration = 800
					}
				}
				30 = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = VIET_province_bridge_collapse
						duration = 1200
					}
				}
				20 = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = VIET_province_bridge_collapse
						duration = 1600
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Reapers"
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = decrease_prosperity_custom_tooltip
				hidden_tooltip = {
					change_variable = { which = prosperity_value value = -7 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Famous Bard refuses to play for the rich
province_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8008
	desc = VIETmisc.8008.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_brothel
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = VIET_famous_bard_province }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 12000
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			NOT = { num_of_max_settlements = 5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			NOT = { num_of_max_settlements = 3 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			owner = {
				is_nomadic = yes
			}
		}
	}
	

	option = { # Arrest him
		name = VIETmisc.8008.a
		owner = {
			random_list = {
				70 = {}
				10 = { add_trait = wroth }
				10 = { add_trait = cruel }
				10 = { add_trait = arbitrary }
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_leader_angered_peasants
				duration = 888
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # OK
		name = VIETmisc.8008.b
		custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_famous_bard_settles }
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = { #randomize how long the bard lives
				20 = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = VIET_famous_bard_province
						duration = 3650
					}
				}
				20 = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = VIET_famous_bard_province
						duration = 5475
					}
				}
				20 = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = VIET_famous_bard_province
						duration = 7300
					}
				}
				20 = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = VIET_famous_bard_province
						duration = 9125
					}
				}
				20 = {
					add_province_modifier = {

				20 = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = VIET_famous_bard_province
						duration = 3650
					}
				}
				20 = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = VIET_famous_bard_province
						duration = 5475
					}
				}
				20 = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = VIET_famous_bard_province
						duration = 7300
					}
				}
				20 = {
					add_province_modifier = {

# Spoopy ship in the skies
province_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8009
	desc = VIETmisc.8009.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_coast_night
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = VIET_province_haunted_ship }
		port = yes
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 12000
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			OR = {
				terrain = steppe
				terrain = arctic
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = {
				OR = {
					is_patrician = yes
					is_merchant_republic = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			NOT = { num_of_max_settlements = 5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			NOT = { num_of_max_settlements = 3 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			owner = {
				OR = {
					is_nomadic = yes
					is_tribal = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	

	option = { # Spoop
		name = VIETmisc.8009.a
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = VIET_province_haunted_ship
			duration = 1095
		}
	}
	option = { # Spoop
		name = VIETmisc.8009.b
		owner = {
			random = {
				add_trait = cynical
				chance = 10
			}		
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = VIET_province_haunted_ship
			duration = 1095
		}
	}
}

# Sandstorm
province_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8011
	desc = VIETmisc.8011.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_sand_desert
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = VIET_province_recent_sandstorm }
		terrain = desert
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 8000
	}
	

	option = { # oh no
		name = VIETmisc.8011.a
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = VIET_province_recent_sandstorm
			duration = 365
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Reapers"
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = decrease_prosperity_custom_tooltip
				hidden_tooltip = {
					change_variable = { which = prosperity_value value = -8 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Suspicious conversation
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8012
	desc = VIETmisc.8012.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		any_courtier = {
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			is_adult = yes
			in_command = no
			is_abroad = no
			OR = {
				trait = ambitious
				trait = proud
			}
			NOT = { trait = diligent }
			NOT = { trait = cynical }
		}
		any_courtier = {
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			is_adult = yes
			in_command = no
			is_abroad = no
			OR = {
				trait = diligent
				trait = cynical
			}
			NOT = { trait = ambitious }
			NOT = { trait = proud }
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}	
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = trusting
		}			
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = content
		}			
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = cruel
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = kind
		}			
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = just
		}			
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			intrigue = 13
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			NOT = { intrigue = 8 }
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				is_adult = yes
				in_command = no
				is_abroad = no
				OR = {
					trait = ambitious
					trait = proud
				}
				NOT = { trait = diligent }
				NOT = { trait = cynical }				
			}
			save_event_target_as = target_VIET_suspicious_courtier_first
		}
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				is_adult = yes
				in_command = no
				is_abroad = no
				OR = {
					trait = diligent
					trait = cynical
				}
				NOT = { trait = ambitious }
				NOT = { trait = proud }			
			}
			save_event_target_as = target_VIET_suspicious_courtier_second
		}		
	}
	
	option = { # suspicious
		name = VIETmisc.8012.a
		event_target:target_VIET_suspicious_courtier_first = {
			opinion = { 
				who = ROOT
				modifier = VIET_opinion_interrupted_secret_conversation
				years = 2
			}		
			reverse_opinion = { 
				who = ROOT
				modifier = VIET_opinion_suspicious_conversation
				years = 2
			}		
		}
		event_target:target_VIET_suspicious_courtier_second = {
			opinion = { 
				who = ROOT
				modifier = VIET_opinion_interrupted_secret_conversation
				years = 2
			}		
			reverse_opinion = { 
				who = ROOT
				modifier = VIET_opinion_suspicious_conversation
				years = 2
			}		
		}		
		random = {
			add_trait = paranoid
			chance = 15
		}		
		random = {
			change_intrigue = 1
			chance = 15
		}
	}
	
	option = { # awkward
		name = VIETmisc.8012.b
		event_target:target_VIET_suspicious_courtier_first = {
			opinion = { 
				who = ROOT
				modifier = VIET_opinion_interrupted_secret_conversation
				years = 1
			}	
		}
		event_target:target_VIET_suspicious_courtier_second = {
			opinion = { 
				who = ROOT
				modifier = VIET_opinion_interrupted_secret_conversation
				years = 1
			}	
		}
		prestige = -5
	}	
	
	option = { # trust
		name = VIETmisc.8012.c
		event_target:target_VIET_suspicious_courtier_first = {
			opinion = { 
				who = ROOT
				modifier = VIET_opinion_interrupted_secret_conversation
				years = 1
			}	
		}
		event_target:target_VIET_suspicious_courtier_second = {
			opinion = { 
				who = ROOT
				modifier = VIET_opinion_interrupted_secret_conversation
				years = 1
			}	
		}
		random = {
			add_trait = trusting
			chance = 20
		}
	}	
	
	option = { # apologize
		name = VIETmisc.8012.d
		random = {
			add_trait = trusting
			chance = 20
		}
	}
}

# Dropped work in poop
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8016
	desc = VIETmisc.8016.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_bad_news

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

		in_command = no
		OR = {
			trait = diligent
			trait = ambitious
		}
		NOT = { trait = slothful }
		NOT = { trait = content }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = trusting
		}

			factor = 1.2
			trait = proud
		}

			factor = 0.8
			trait = humble
		}			
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = arbitrary
		}			
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = greedy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = temperate
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Touch poop
		name = VIETmisc.8016.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_touched_poop
			duration = 365
		}
		random = {
			add_trait = stressed
			chance = 33
		}
	}	
	option = { # Being Type A is bad, don't be Type A!
		name = VIETmisc.8016.b
		piety = 5
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = ambitious
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = ambitious
				chance = 30
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = diligent
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = diligent
				chance = 30
			}
		}
	}		
	option = { # Scribe made copies
		name = VIETmisc.8016.c
		tooltip_info = learning
		trigger = {
			learning = 13
			NOT = { trait = genius }
			NOT = { trait = quick }
			NOT = { trait = shrewd }
		}
	}			
	option = { # Scribe made copies
		name = VIETmisc.8016.c
		tooltip_info = genius
		trigger = {
			trait = genius
		}
	}			
	option = { # Scribe made copies
		name = VIETmisc.8016.c
		tooltip_info = quick
		trigger = {
			trait = quick
		}
	}				
	option = { # Scribe made copies
		name = VIETmisc.8016.c
		tooltip_info = shrewd
		trigger = {
			trait = shrewd
		}
	}

# Rumors of a Chinese women playing polo
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8018
	desc = VIETmisc.8018.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_chinese_princess
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		#Where people play polo
		OR = {
			culture_group = altaic
			culture_group = iranian
			culture_group = arabic
			culture_group = byzantine
			culture_group = indoaryan
			culture_group = dravidian

# Meet an amazing singer - will she join us?
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8021
	desc = VIETmisc.8021.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_maiden

	option = { # she won't join us - okay
		name = VIETmisc.8021.a
	}	
	option = { # she won't join us - her loss
		name = VIETmisc.8021.b
		piety = -5
		random_list = {
			10 = { add_trait = wroth }
			20 = { add_trait = proud }
			70 = {}
		}
	}		
	option = { # she will join us... for a price
		name = VIETmisc.8021.c
		set_character_flag = VIET_amazing_singer_invite
		wealth = -20
		custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_offer_money_to_singer }
		hidden_tooltip = {			
			create_character = {
				age = 18
				dynasty = random
				religion = ROOT
				culture = ROOT
				female = yes
				health = 5
				random_traits = no
				historical = yes
				attributes = {
					diplomacy = 8
					martial = 5
					stewardship = 5
					intrigue = 5
					learning = 6
				}
			}
			new_character = {
				#Education & other basic stuff
				save_event_target_as = VIET_amazing_singer
				add_character_modifier = {
					name = VIET_amazing_singer_modifier
					duration = -1
				}
				set_character_flag = ai_flag_refuse_concubinage
				set_character_flag = ai_flag_refuse_marriage
				set_character_flag = VIET_amazing_singer
				reverse_opinion = { 
					who = ROOT
					modifier = VIET_opinion_amazing_court_singer
					years = 100
				}
				set_character_flag = no_court_invites
				random_list = {
					50 = { add_trait = charismatic_negotiator }
					25 = { add_trait = grey_eminence }
					15 = { add_trait = scholarly_theologian }
					10 = { add_trait = mastermind_theologian }
				}	
				#Guaranteed Traits
				add_trait = poet
				add_trait = fair
				#add_trait = melodious_voice
				add_trait = kind
				add_trait = chaste
				#Clutter Artifact					
				random = {
					VIET_give_clutter_artifact_effect = yes
					chance = 10
				}
				#Flavor
				random_list = {
					70 = { } #Nothing
					25 = { add_scarred_tiered_effect = yes }
					5 = { 
						trigger = { has_dlc = Reapers }
						add_trait = one_eyed
					}
				}
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_loyal_servant
					who = ROOT
					years = 100
				}			
				if = {
					limit = { has_dlc = "Way of Life" }
					random_list = {
						60 = { add_trait = socializer }
						10 = { add_trait = scholar }
						10 = { add_trait = seductress }
						20 = {}
					}
				}
				#Personality Archetypes
				random_list = {
					20 = { # Sassy girl
						set_character_flag = VIET_singer_sassy
						add_trait = cynical
						add_trait = erudite
						add_trait = stubborn
					}
					20 = { # Social climber
						set_character_flag = VIET_singer_ambitions
						add_trait = proud
						add_trait = diligent
						add_trait = ambitious
					}
					20 = { # Wallflower
						set_character_flag = VIET_singer_wallflower
						add_trait = shy
						add_trait = humble
						add_trait = slothful
					}
					20 = { # tomboy
						set_character_flag = VIET_singer_tomboy
						add_trait = brave
						add_trait = gregarious
						add_trait = wroth
					}
					20 = { # religious
						set_character_flag = VIET_singer_pious
						add_trait = zealous
						add_trait = temperate
						add_trait = charitable
					}
				}
			}
			#Make husbando
			create_character = {
				age = 21
				dynasty = actually_culture
				religion = ROOT
				culture = ROOT
				female = no
				health = 5
				random_traits = no
				historical= yes
				attributes = {
					diplomacy = 6
					martial = 5
					stewardship = 6
					intrigue = 5
					learning = 6
				}
			}
			new_character = {
				add_spouse = event_target:VIET_amazing_singer
				add_lover = event_target:VIET_amazing_singer
				add_friend = event_target:VIET_amazing_singer
				set_character_flag = ai_flag_refuse_concubinage
				set_character_flag = ai_flag_refuse_marriage
				set_character_flag = VIET_amazing_singer_husband
				set_character_flag = no_court_invites
				add_character_modifier = {
					name = VIET_amazing_singer_husbando_modifier
					duration = -1
				}
				#Guaranteed Traits
				add_trait = fair
				#add_trait = tall
				add_trait = kind
				add_trait = chaste

					VIET_give_clutter_artifact_effect = yes
					chance = 10
				}
				#Flavor
				random_list = {
					70 = { } #Nothing
					25 = { add_scarred_tiered_effect = yes }
					5 = { 
						trigger = { has_dlc = Reapers }
						add_trait = one_eyed
						change_martial = 1
					}
				}
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_loyal_servant
					who = ROOT
					years = 100
				}
				#Personality Archetypes
				random_list = {
					20 = { # Good soldier
						set_character_flag = VIET_singer_husband_soldier

						add_trait = honest
						add_trait = temperate
						random_list = {
							40 = { add_trait = tough_soldier }
							40 = { add_trait = skilled_tactician }

			trait = diligent
		}

			trait = gregarious

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = cruel
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = proud
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = VIET_spirited_chinese_lady_visits 
	}

	}

		}

			trait = slothful

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = charitable
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = greedy
		}
	}

		name = VIETmisc.8043.a
		prestige = -1
	}

		name = VIETmisc.8043.b

			10 = { add_trait = ambitious }
			20 = { add_trait = stubborn }
			70 = { }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ill = no
				NOT = {
					has_dlc = "Reapers"
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				75 = { }
				25 = { add_trait = ill }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ill = no
				has_dlc = "Reapers"
			}
			
			random_list = {
				50 = { }
				50 = { 
					set_character_flag = disease_not_serious
					add_trait = vomiting
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = RIP.11005 days = 15 random = 10 } }
		}
	}

		}

			trait = diligent
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = cruel
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = trusting
		}
	}

	
	option = { # soft
		name = VIETmisc.8044.a
		piety = 1
	}		
	option = { # hard
		name = VIETmisc.8044.b
		prestige = 1
	}		
	option = { # either is fine
		name = VIETmisc.8044.c
		random_list = {
			50 = { piety = 1 }
			50 = { prestige = 1 }
		}
	}		
	option = { # abstain from eggs for a while
		name = VIETmisc.8044.d
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = muslim
			}
			decadence = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = gluttonous
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = gluttonous
				chance = 40
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				add_trait = temperate
				chance = 15
			}
		}
	}	
}

# Pistachios
province_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8049
	desc = VIETmisc.8049.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_moorish_decor
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = VIET_province_pistachios }
		owner = {
			is_nomadic = no
			is_tribal = no
		}
		OR = {
			region = world_middle_east
			region = world_persia
			region = world_europe_south
			region = world_europe_west_iberia
			region = world_africa_north
			region = world_asia_minor
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 10000
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			NOT = { num_of_max_settlements = 5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			NOT = { num_of_max_settlements = 3 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.3

					duration = 7300
				}				
			}
			30 = {
				add_province_modifier = {

				}				
			}
			20 = {
				add_province_modifier = {

			}

character_event = {

	war = no

		is_nomadic = no
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
			
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			is_strong_trigger = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			is_weak_trigger = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = arbitrary
		}
	}

	
	option = { # Carry on
		name = VIETmisc.8054.a
		prestige = 5
	}	
	option = { # Working class scum!
		name = VIETmisc.8054.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = humble
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = humble
				chance = 60
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				add_trait = proud
				chance = 25
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = trusting
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = trusting
				chance = 40
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				add_trait = paranoid
				chance = 25
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = muslim
			}
			decadence = 1
		}
	}		
	option = { # Talk to the commoners
		name = VIETmisc.8054.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { trait = shy }
		}
		prestige = -5
		random_list = {
			15 = { add_trait = gregarious }
			10 = { add_trait = just }
			10 = { add_trait = humble }
			65 = {}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = muslim
			}
			decadence = -1
		}
	}	
}

				religion_group = muslim
			}
			random = {
				decadence = -1
				chance = 25
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Glory
		name = VIETmisc.8059.d
		random_list = {
			15 = { add_trait = ambitious }
			15 = { add_trait = diligent }
			15 = { add_trait = stubborn }
			15 = { add_trait = gregarious }
			40 = {}
		}
	}	
}

			trait = lustful
		}

			factor = 0.8

			factor = 1.2
			trait = gluttonous
		}

			factor = 0.8
			trait = temperate
		}

			name = VIET_moved_to_tears

		}

			limit = {
				age = 10
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				NOT = { trait = cynical }
				NOT = { trait = brooding }
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_moved_to_tears
				duration = 543
			}
		}
		any_courtier = {
			limit = {
				age = 10
				OR = {
					trait = brooding
					trait = cynical
				}
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_emotionless_to_art
				duration = 543
			}
		}
	}	
	option = { # I don't cry
		name = VIETmisc.8060.b
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_emotionless_to_art
			duration = 543
		}
		any_courtier = {
			limit = {
				age = 10
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				NOT = { trait = cynical }
				NOT = { trait = brooding }
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_moved_to_tears
				duration = 543
			}
		}

				}
			}

			}
		}
	}	
}


# Auriel's Ascension - deity manifests themselves
province_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8061
	title = VIETmisc.8061.title
	desc = VIETmisc.8061.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_holy_light
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = VIET_auriels_ascension }
		owner = {
			is_nomadic = no
			religion = ROOT
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 12000
	}

	
	option = { # Nice
		name = VIETmisc.8061.a
		owner = {
			piety = 5
			if = {
				limit = {
					trait = cynical
				}
				random = {
					remove_trait = cynical
					chance = 80
				}
			}
			else = {
				random = {
					add_trait = zealous
					chance = 30
				}
			}		
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = VIET_auriels_ascension
			duration = 12580
		}
	}	
	option = { # It's a cult!
		name = VIETmisc.8061.b
		owner = {
			prestige = 10
			random = {
				add_trait = zealous
				chance = 75
			}		
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = VIET_repressing_cult
			duration = 4000
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = VIET_auriels_ascension
			duration = 4000
		}
	}	
	option = { # No opinion
		name = VIETmisc.8061.c
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = VIET_auriels_ascension
			duration = 8250
		}
	}	
}

	}

			trait = diligent
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = greedy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = gregarious
		}
	}

	
	option = { # Will wait
		name = VIETmisc.8062.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = wroth
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = wroth
				chance = 40
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				add_trait = patient
				chance = 50
			}
		}
	}	
	option = { # How dare he!
		name = VIETmisc.8062.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = patient
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = patient
				chance = 65
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			25 = { add_trait = wroth }
			25 = { add_trait = cynical }
			15 = { add_trait = paranoid }
			35 = { }
		}
	}	
	option = { # Can't do much about it
		name = VIETmisc.8062.c
		random_list = {
			20 = { add_trait = content }
			20 = { add_trait = humble }
			20 = { add_trait = patient }
			40 = { }
		}
	}	
}

# Enter the WW1 / World War 1 dream
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8065
	desc = VIETmisc.8065.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_nightmare
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
	
	trigger = {
		#in_command = no
		NOT = { # A fairly serious event, but dreaming of WW1 might be immersion breaking for some
			has_game_rule = {
				name = VIET_events_rules
				value = serious
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_great_war_dream }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
			
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			war = yes
		}			
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			war = no
		}			
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = depressed
		}			
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = stressed
		}			
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = erudite
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = wroth
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = honest
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = VIET_great_war_dream
	}
	
	option = { # Okay
		name = VIETmisc.8065.a
		narrative_event = { id = VIETmisc.8066 tooltip = VIETmisc.8066.tooltip }
	}	
}

# Dreaming of your realm's future
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8070
	desc = VIETmisc.8070.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_tuscan_country
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
	
	trigger = {
		#in_command = no
		NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_future_dream_cool }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
			
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = cynical
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = humble
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = VIET_future_dream_cool
	}
	
	# Actual choice of direction doesn't matter, only thing that matters is if character has enough good vs bad traits
	# Also practicing the application of calc_true_if
	
	option = { # Go right
		name = VIETmisc.8070.a
		if = { #if you're a dick
			limit = {
				calc_true_if = {
					amount = 3
					trait = envious
					trait = greedy
					trait = lustful
					trait = proud
					trait = slothful
					trait = wroth
					trait = gluttonous
					trait = arbitrary
					trait = ambitious
					trait = craven
					trait = cruel
					trait = impaler
					trait = hedonist
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				random_list = {
					75 = { character_event = { id = VIETmisc.8071 } }
					25 = { character_event = { id = VIETmisc.8072 } }
				}			
			}
			break = yes # Skip tombola, you're done!
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				calc_true_if = {
					amount = 3
					trait = kind
					trait = charitable
					trait = chaste
					trait = humble
					trait = diligent
					trait = patient
					trait = temperate
					trait = just
					trait = content
					trait = brave
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				random_list = {
					25 = { character_event = { id = VIETmisc.8071 } }
					75 = { character_event = { id = VIETmisc.8072 } }
				}			
			}
			break = yes # Skip tombola, you're done!
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = { character_event = { id = VIETmisc.8071 } }
				50 = { character_event = { id = VIETmisc.8072 } }
			}		
		}
	}	
	option = { # Go left
		name = VIETmisc.8070.b
		if = { #if you're a dick
			limit = {
				calc_true_if = {
					amount = 3
					trait = envious
					trait = greedy
					trait = lustful
					trait = proud
					trait = slothful
					trait = wroth
					trait = gluttonous
					trait = arbitrary
					trait = ambitious
					trait = craven
					trait = cruel
					trait = impaler
					trait = hedonist
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				random_list = {
					75 = { character_event = { id = VIETmisc.8071 } }
					25 = { character_event = { id = VIETmisc.8072 } }
				}			
			}
			break = yes # Skip tombola, you're done!
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				calc_true_if = {
					amount = 3
					trait = kind
					trait = charitable
					trait = chaste
					trait = humble
					trait = diligent
					trait = patient
					trait = temperate
					trait = just
					trait = content
					trait = brave
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				random_list = {
					25 = { character_event = { id = VIETmisc.8071 } }
					75 = { character_event = { id = VIETmisc.8072 } }
				}			
			}
			break = yes # Skip tombola, you're done!
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = { character_event = { id = VIETmisc.8071 } }
				50 = { character_event = { id = VIETmisc.8072 } }
			}		
		}
	}	
}

			factor = 1.2

		}

# Monk claiming to be Maitreya, the Buddha at end times, starts a cult
province_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8075
	desc = VIETmisc.8075.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_monk_eastern_group
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = VIET_maitreya_cult }
		owner = {
			is_nomadic = no
			OR = {
				religion_group = bud_group
				religion = tao
				religion = tao_reformed
				is_sinosphere_small_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		religion_group = bud_group
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 10000
		modifier = { #less likely when China's stable if in non-Indian territory
			factor = 2
			NOT = {
				region = world_india
			}
			offmap_china = {
				NOR = {
					has_status = china_civil_war
					has_status = china_plague
					has_status = china_mongol_invasion
					has_status = china_jurchen_invasion
					has_status = china_unrest
				}			
			}
		}
		#modifier = {
		#	factor = 1.5
		#	NOT = { num_of_max_settlements = 5 }
		#}
		#modifier = {
		#	factor = 1.2
		#	NOT = { num_of_max_settlements = 3 }
		#}
	}
	

	option = { # Imprison and oppress cult
		name = VIETmisc.8075.a
		custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_maitreya_cult_imprison }
		owner = {
			prestige = 10
			piety = 10
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = VIET_repressing_cult
			duration = 4000
		}
	}
	option = { # Execute and oppress cult
		name = VIETmisc.8075.b
		custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_maitreya_cult_execute }
		owner = {
			prestige = 20
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = VIET_repressing_cult
			duration = 3000
		}
	}
	option = { # Let him go
		name = VIETmisc.8075.c
		custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_maitreya_cult_release }
		owner = {
			prestige = -20
			piety = -10
			random_list = {
				15 = { add_trait = slothful }
				15 = { add_trait = content }
				15 = { add_trait = cynical }
				15 = { add_trait = arbitrary }
				40 = { }
			}
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = VIET_maitreya_cult
			duration = 5555
		}
	}
	option = { # Public debate
		name = VIETmisc.8075.d
		custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_maitreya_cult_debate }
		owner = {
			wealth = -20
			prestige = 15
			piety = 15
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = VIET_maitreya_cult
			duration = 2085
		}
	}
}

# Courtier eats food too fast and is warned about it
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8078
	desc = VIETmisc.8078.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_feast_hf
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
		
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_dont_choke_lol }
		any_courtier = {
			ai = yes
			is_adult = yes
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			OR = {
				trait = gluttonous
				trait = slothful
				trait = wroth
				trait = paranoid
				is_dumb_trigger = yes
			}
			in_command = no
			is_abroad = no
			NOT = { trait = temperate }
			NOT = { trait = patient }
			#prevent important relatives and spouses from dying
			NOT = { is_consort = ROOT }
			NOT = { is_close_relative = ROOT }
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = paranoid
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = deceitful
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = VIET_dont_choke_lol 
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				ai = yes
				is_adult = yes
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				OR = {
					trait = gluttonous
					trait = slothful
					trait = wroth
					trait = paranoid
					is_dumb_trigger = yes
				}
				in_command = no
				is_abroad = no
				NOT = { trait = temperate }
				NOT = { trait = patient }
				#prevent important relatives and spouses from dying
				NOT = { is_consort = ROOT }
				NOT = { is_close_relative = ROOT }			
			}
			save_event_target_as = target_VIET_choking_warning_courtier
		}	
	}
	
	option = { # Ignore their problem
		name = VIETmisc.8078.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = kind
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = kind
				chance = 45
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random = {
				event_target:target_VIET_choking_warning_courtier = {
					set_character_flag = VIET_marked_for_choking_death
				}
				chance = 50
			}
			character_event = { id = VIETmisc.8079 days = 30 random = 60 }
		}
	}	
	
	option = { # Tell them to be careful - will decrease chances of death!
		name = VIETmisc.8078.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = envious
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = envious
				chance = 40
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				add_trait = kind
				chance = 25
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random = {
				event_target:target_VIET_choking_warning_courtier = {
					set_character_flag = VIET_marked_for_choking_death
				}
				chance = 25
			}
			character_event = { id = VIETmisc.8079 days = 30 random = 60 }
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Use diplomacy to tell them - will prevent them from dying
		name = VIETmisc.8078.c
		tooltip_info = diplomacy
		trigger = {
			diplomacy = 10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = envious
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = envious
				chance = 40
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				add_trait = kind
				chance = 25
			}
		}
		event_target:target_VIET_choking_warning_courtier = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_reasonable_advice
				who = ROOT
				years = 4
			}				
		}
	}	
}


# Courtier chokes - possibly to death
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8079
	desc = VIETmisc.8079.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_feast_hf
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { # Uh oh!
		name = VIETmisc.8079.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:target_VIET_choking_warning_courtier = {
					has_character_flag = VIET_marked_for_choking_death
				}
			}
			event_target:target_VIET_choking_warning_courtier = {
				death = {
					death_reason = death_VIET_choking_food
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			event_target:target_VIET_choking_warning_courtier = {
				prestige = -5
			}
		}
	}	
}

# What to do when I'm a grown up?
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8081
	desc = VIETmisc.8081.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_garden
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 4
	max_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
		
	trigger = {
		#in_command = no
		NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_what_do_when_grown_up }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			age = 9
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = VIET_what_do_when_grown_up
	}
	
	option = { # Adventure
		name = VIETmisc.8081.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Zeus"
			}
			random_list = {
				10 = { add_trait = curious }
				10 = { add_trait = playful }
				10 = { add_trait = willful }
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_list = {
				10 = { add_trait = brave }
				10 = { add_trait = gregarious }
				10 = { add_trait = greedy }
			}	
		}
		random_list = {
			10 = { change_martial = 1 }
			10 = { change_learning = 1 }
			10 = { change_diplomacy = 1 }
		}
	}		
	option = { # Do forbidden things
		name = VIETmisc.8081.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Zeus"
			}
			random_list = {
				10 = { add_trait = haughty }
				10 = { add_trait = rowdy }
				10 = { add_trait = fussy }
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_list = {
				10 = { add_trait = lustful }
				10 = { add_trait = cynical }
				10 = { add_trait = gluttonous }
			}	
		}
		random_list = {
			10 = { change_martial = 1 }
			10 = { change_learning = 1 }
			10 = { change_intrigue = 1 }
		}
	}		
	option = { # Not make trouble
		name = VIETmisc.8081.c
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Zeus"
			}
			random_list = {
				10 = { add_trait = timid }
				10 = { add_trait = indolent	}
				10 = { add_trait = affectionate }
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_list = {
				10 = { add_trait = shy }
				10 = { add_trait = kind }
				10 = { add_trait = humble }
			}	
		}
		random_list = {
			10 = { change_stewardship = 1 }
			10 = { change_learning = 1 }
			10 = { change_diplomacy = 1 }
		}
	}			
	option = { # Become a good ruler
		name = VIETmisc.8081.d
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Zeus"
			}
			random_list = {
				10 = { add_trait = idolizer }
				10 = { add_trait = conscientious }
				10 = { add_trait = brooding }
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_list = {
				10 = { add_trait = just }
				10 = { add_trait = diligent }
				10 = { add_trait = honest }
			}	
		}
		random_list = {
			10 = { change_martial = 1 }
			10 = { change_stewardship = 1 }
			10 = { change_diplomacy = 1 }
		}
	}	
}

		}

			factor = 1.2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			is_weak_trigger = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			is_strong_trigger = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = honest
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Rest
		name = VIETmisc.8082.a
		prestige = -5
		if  = {
			limit = {
				trait = diligent
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = diligent
				chance = 45
			}
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				trait = ambitious
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = ambitious
				chance = 25
			}
		}
	}		
	option = { # Continue on!
		name = VIETmisc.8083.a
		random = {
			add_trait = stressed
			chance = 25
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_tiring_travel
			duration = 642
		}
	}	
}

# Courtier stared at sun for too long
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8089
	desc = VIETmisc.8089.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_apollo_sun
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no
		
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		any_courtier = {
			ai = yes
			is_adult = yes
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			in_command = no
			is_abroad = no
			OR = {
				is_dumb_trigger = yes
				trait = stubborn
				trait = ambitious
				trait = slothful
				trait = wroth
				#trait = absentminded
			}
			NOR = {
				trait = content
				trait = patient
				is_smart_trigger = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		
		modifier = { #don't want it to happen too often
			factor = 0.05
			any_courtier = {
				has_character_modifier = VIET_permanent_sun_damage
			}
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = cruel
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = kind
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = honest
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Stupid
		name = VIETmisc.8089.a
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				ai = yes
				is_adult = yes
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				in_command = no
				is_abroad = no
				OR = {
					is_dumb_trigger = yes
					trait = stubborn
					trait = ambitious
					trait = slothful
					trait = wroth
					#trait = absentminded
				}
				NOR = {
					trait = content
					trait = patient
					is_smart_trigger = yes
				}			
			}
			random_list = {
				45 = {
					add_character_modifier = {
						name = VIET_stared_at_sun
						duration = 450
					}
				}
				30 = {
					add_character_modifier = {
						name = VIET_stared_at_sun
						duration = 900
					}
				}
				25 = {
					add_character_modifier = {
						name = VIET_permanent_sun_damage
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}	
}

		owner = {

		}
		NOT = { terrain = desert }
		NOT = { terrain = arctic }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 8000
	}
	

	option = { # Spend funds to help
		name = VIETmisc.8093.a
		owner = {
			wealth = -20
			piety = 10
			prestige = 10
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = VIET_province_giant_shade_tree
			duration = 10950
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Reapers"
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = increase_prosperity_custom_tooltip
				hidden_tooltip = {					
					change_variable = { which = prosperity_value value = 10 }
				}
			}
		}
	}	
	option = { # Don't help
		name = VIETmisc.8093.b
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = VIET_province_giant_shade_tree
			duration = 3650
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Reapers"
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = increase_prosperity_custom_tooltip
				hidden_tooltip = {					
					change_variable = { which = prosperity_value value = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
	}	
}


# Shadows attack villagers - implied to be hysteria from several cases of sleep paralysis
province_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8094
	desc = VIETmisc.8094.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_village_at_night
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = VIET_province_shadow_hysteria }
		owner = {
			is_nomadic = no
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 8000
	}
	

	option = { # Troubling!
		name = VIETmisc.8094.a
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = VIET_province_shadow_hysteria
			duration = 730
		}
	}
	option = { # Send in clergy to pray
		name = VIETmisc.8094.b
		owner = {
			wealth = -5
			piety = 5
		}
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = VIET_province_shadow_hysteria
					duration = 365
				}			
			}
			25 = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = VIET_province_shadow_hysteria
					duration = 730
				}			
			}
			25 = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = VIET_province_shadow_hysteria
					duration = 1095
				}			
			}
		}
	}	
	option = { # Commoners are making things up
		name = VIETmisc.8094.c
		owner = {
			random = {
				add_trait = cynical
				chance = 25
			}
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = VIET_province_shadow_hysteria
			duration = 730
		}
	}		
	option = { # Scholars know this is night terror
		name = VIETmisc.8094.d
		tooltip_info = learning
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				learning = 11
				NOT = { trait = scholar }
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			75 = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = VIET_province_shadow_hysteria
					duration = 365
				}			
			}
			25 = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = VIET_province_shadow_hysteria
					duration = 730
				}			
			}
		}		
	}		
	option = { # Scholars know this is night terror
		name = VIETmisc.8094.d
		tooltip_info = scholar
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				trait = scholar
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			75 = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = VIET_province_shadow_hysteria
					duration = 365
				}			
			}
			25 = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = VIET_province_shadow_hysteria
					duration = 730
				}			
			}
		}		
	}	
}




# Someone at the market wears a black hoodie
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8095
	desc = VIETmisc.8095.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_market_hf
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no
		
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = craven
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = envious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = kind
		}
	}
	
	option = { # false alarm
		name = VIETmisc.8095.a
		random_list = {
			50 = { prestige = -1 }
			50 = { piety = -1 }
		}
	}	
	option = { # suspicious...
		name = VIETmisc.8095.b
		random_list = {
			50 = { prestige = -1 }
			50 = { piety = -1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = trusting
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = trusting
				chance = 70
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				add_trait = paranoid
				chance = 55
			}
		}		
	}	
}

# Found a nice secret hiding spot
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8098
	desc = VIETmisc.8098.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_garden
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no
		
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = craven
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = cruel
		}
	}
	
	option = { # visit by myself
		name = VIETmisc.8098.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = gregarious
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = gregarious
				chance = 80
			}
		}
		health = 0.5
		piety = 10
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_secret_relax_spot
			duration = 1825
		}
	}	
	option = { # go with people
		name = VIETmisc.8098.b
		prestige = 10
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = shy
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = shy
				chance = 75
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				add_trait = gregarious
				chance = 75
			}
		}
		any_courtier = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_showed_secret_relax_spot
				who = ROOT
				years = 10
			}			
		}
	}
	option = { # go with lover
		name = VIETmisc.8098.b
		trigger = {
			has_lover = yes
			any_lover = {
				is_pregnant = no
				is_female = yes
				NOR = {
					trait = incapable
					age = 45
				}
				is_abroad = no
				in_command = no	
			}
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_secret_relax_spot_sexy
			duration = 1095
		}
		random_lover = {
			limit = {
				is_pregnant = no
				is_female = yes
				NOR = {
					trait = incapable
					age = 45
				}
				is_abroad = no
				in_command = no	
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_showed_secret_relax_spot_lover
				who = ROOT
				years = 10
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_secret_relax_spot_sexy
				duration = 1095
			}
			random = {
				chance = 30
				impregnate = ROOT
			}			
		}
	}	
}



# Fun in the sun
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8099
	desc = VIETmisc.8099.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_tropicana
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no
		
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		capital_scope = {
			port = yes
			#Warm tropical region
			OR = {
				region = world_africa
				region = world_india
				region = world_middle_east
				region = world_persia
				region = world_asia_minor
				region = world_europe_south
				region = world_europe_west_iberia
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = wroth
		}
	}
	
	option = { # visit by myself
		name = VIETmisc.8099.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_fun_in_the_sun
			duration = 365
		}
	}	
	option = { # go with family
		name = VIETmisc.8099.b
		trigger = {
			any_courtier = {
				is_close_relative = ROOT
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				is_abroad = no
				in_command = no
			}
		}
		any_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_close_relative = ROOT
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				is_abroad = no
				in_command = no			
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_beach_trip
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
			reverse_opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_beach_trip
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_fun_in_the_sun
				duration = 365
			}			
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_fun_in_the_sun
			duration = 365
		}
	}
	option = { # get to know courtier
		name = VIETmisc.8099.c
		trigger = {
			any_courtier = {
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 }
				is_abroad = no
				in_command = no
			}
		}
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 }
				is_abroad = no
				in_command = no	
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_beach_trip
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
			reverse_opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_beach_trip
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_fun_in_the_sun
				duration = 365
			}
			random = {
				add_friend = ROOT
				chance = 40
			}
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_fun_in_the_sun
			duration = 365
		}
	}
	option = { # go with lover
		name = VIETmisc.8099.d
		trigger = {
			has_lover = yes
			any_lover = {
				is_pregnant = no
				is_female = yes
				NOR = {
					trait = incapable
					age = 45
				}
				is_abroad = no
				in_command = no	
			}
		}
		random_lover = {
			limit = {
				is_pregnant = no
				is_female = yes
				NOR = {
					trait = incapable
					age = 45
				}
				is_abroad = no
				in_command = no	
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_beach_trip

				years = 1
			}
			reverse_opinion = {

# Youths prank a village, pretending to be shadow demons
province_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8101
	desc = VIETmisc.8101.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_judged_by_ruler
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = VIET_province_youth_prank }
		owner = {
			is_nomadic = no
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 10000
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			NOT = { num_of_max_settlements = 5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			NOT = { num_of_max_settlements = 3 }
		}
	}
	

	option = { # Who cares
		name = VIETmisc.8101.a
		owner = {
			random = {
				add_trait = arbitrary
				chance = 30
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trait = wroth
				}
				random = {
					remove_trait = wroth
					chance = 75
				}
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = the_merciful
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = VIET_province_youth_prank
			duration = 365
		}
	}

	option = { # Public Humiliation
		name = VIETmisc.8101.b
		owner = {
			prestige = 10
			random = {
				add_trait = just
				chance = 20
			}
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = VIET_province_youth_prank
			duration = 365
		}
	}

	option = { # Imprison!
		name = VIETmisc.8101.c
		owner = {
			prestige = 5
			random_list = {
				30 = { add_trait = just }
				20 = { add_trait = wroth }
				50 = { }
			}
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = VIET_province_youth_prank
			duration = 365
		}
	}

	option = { # Execute!
		name = VIETmisc.8101.d
		owner = {
			random_list = {
				50 = { add_trait = cruel }
				35 = { add_trait = wroth }
				15 = { add_trait = arbitrary }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trait = kind
				}
				remove_trait = kind
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trait = just
				}
				random = {
					remove_trait = just
					chance = 60
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trait = patient
				}
				random = {
					remove_trait = patient
					chance = 30
				}
			}
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = VIET_province_youth_prank
			duration = 365
		}
	}
}


# Astronomer presents a star chart
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8102
	desc = VIETmisc.8102.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_comet
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no
		
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		NOT = { has_artifact = VIET_star_chart }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
			
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.3
			viet_artifact_loss_three_flags = yes
		}				
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.3
			any_artifact = {
				has_artifact_flag = VIET_clutter_flag
			}
		}			
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = erudite
		}
		modifier = {

# Child wants a midnight snack
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8104
	desc = VIETmisc.8104.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_artemis_moon
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 4
	max_age = 14

	#trigger = {
	#	has_guardian = yes
	#}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = playful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = indolent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = fussy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = timid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = rowdy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = conscientious
		}
	}
	
	option = { # go get food
		name = VIETmisc.8104.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Zeus"
			}
			random_list = {
				25 = { add_trait = playful }
				25 = { add_trait = willful }
				25 = { add_trait = conscientious }
				25 = { }
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_list = {
				25 = { add_trait = humble }
				25 = { add_trait = brave }
				25 = { add_trait = gregarious }
				25 = { }
			}	
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Call a servant
		name = VIETmisc.8104.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Zeus"
			}
			random_list = {
				25 = { add_trait = fussy }
				25 = { add_trait = haughty }
				25 = { add_trait = rowdy }
				25 = { }
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_list = {
				25 = { add_trait = slothful }
				25 = { add_trait = proud }
				25 = { add_trait = gluttonous }
				25 = { }
			}	
		}
	}	
	
	option = { # no
		name = VIETmisc.8104.c
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Zeus"
			}
			random_list = {
				25 = { add_trait = indolent }
				25 = { add_trait = timid }
				25 = { add_trait = brooding }
				25 = { }
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_list = {
				25 = { add_trait = patient }
				25 = { add_trait = craven }
				25 = { add_trait = temperate }
				25 = { }
			}	
		}
	}	
	
	option = { # watch the night sky
		name = VIETmisc.8104.d
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Zeus"
			}
			random_list = {
				25 = { add_trait = idolizer }
				25 = { add_trait = curious }
				25 = { add_trait = affectionate }
				25 = { }
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_list = {
				25 = { add_trait = erudite }
				25 = { add_trait = kind }
				25 = { add_trait = zealous }
				25 = { }
			}	
		}
	}	
}

# Ghostly apparitions no longer appear after sunset
province_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8106
	desc = VIETmisc.8106.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_artemis_moon
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = VIET_province_night_ghosts_disappear }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 10000
		#modifier = {
		#	factor = 1.5
		#	NOT = { num_of_max_settlements = 5 }
		#}
		#modifier = {
		#	factor = 1.2
		#	NOT = { num_of_max_settlements = 3 }
		#}
	}
	

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.8106.a
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = VIET_province_night_ghosts_disappear
			duration = 666
		}
	}	

	option = { # doubt
		name = VIETmisc.8106.b
		owner = {
			random_list = {
				20 = { add_trait = brave }
				20 = { add_trait = cynical }
				10 = { add_trait = proud }
				50 = { }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trait = craven
				}
				random = {
					remove_trait = craven
					chance = 40
				}
			}
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = VIET_province_night_ghosts_disappear
			duration = 666
		}
	}	

	option = { # celebrate
		name = VIETmisc.8106.c
		owner = {
			random_list = {
				20 = { add_trait = content }
				10 = { add_trait = trusting }
				10 = { add_trait = patient }
				50 = { }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trait = craven
				}
				random = {
					remove_trait = craven
					chance = 30
				}
			}
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = VIET_province_night_ghosts_disappear
			duration = 666
		}
	}
}

				has_artifact_flag = VIET_clutter_flag
			}
		}			
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = ambitious
		}

			factor = 0.8
			trait = content
		}

			factor = 1.2
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = cynical
		}
	}
	
	option = { # hunt them down
		name = VIETmisc.8112.a
		wealth = -10
		prestige = -5
		piety = 5
		random_list = {
			25 = { add_trait = just }
			15 = { add_trait = diligent }
			10 = { add_trait = zealous }
			50 = { }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = muslim
			}
			decadence = -1
		}
		narrative_event = { id = VIETmisc.8113 tooltip = VIETmisc.8113.tooltip days = 2 random = 10 }
	}	
	option = { # don't care
		name = VIETmisc.8112.b
		piety = -5
		prestige = -5
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = just
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = just
				chance = 66
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				add_trait = slothful
				chance = 25
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = muslim
			}
			decadence = 1
		}
	}
}

		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_sobering_lesson
			duration = 365
		}
		
		any_courtier = {
			limit = {
				age = 10
				NOT = { trait = ambitious }
				NOT = { trait = cruel }
				NOT = { trait = cynical }
				NOT = { trait = proud }
				NOT = { trait = haughty }
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_sobering_lesson
				duration = 365
			}		
		}
		
	}	
	
	option = { # weakling!
		name = VIETmisc.8114.b

		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_no_empathy
			duration = 365
		}
		
		any_courtier = {
			limit = {
				age = 10
				NOT = { trait = ambitious }
				NOT = { trait = cruel }
				NOT = { trait = cynical }
				NOT = { trait = proud }
				NOT = { trait = haughty }
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_sobering_lesson
				duration = 365
			}		
		}
		
	}
	
	option = { # Imprison the friend!
		name = VIETmisc.8114.c
		
		prestige = 10
		
		random_list = {
			20 = { add_trait = arbitrary }
			20 = { add_trait = wroth }
			20 = { add_trait = just }
			40 = { }
		}

		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_sobering_lesson
			duration = 365
		}
		
		any_courtier = {
			limit = {
				age = 10
				NOT = { trait = ambitious }
				NOT = { trait = cruel }
				NOT = { trait = cynical }
				NOT = { trait = proud }
				NOT = { trait = haughty }
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_sobering_lesson
				duration = 365
			}		
		}
		
	}
	
}

# Hunted a wolf and find a nice wolf pelt
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8116
	desc = VIETmisc.8116.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_wolf
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no
		
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		NAND = {
			OR = {
				religion_group = bud_group
				religion = jain
			}
			OR = {
				trait = zealous
				trait = kind
				trait = just
			}
			NOT = { trait = cynical }
		}
		health = 4
		#Wolves aren't found everywhere (based on Wikipedia's page on wolves)
		capital_scope = {
			NOR = {
				region = world_africa
				region = world_india_south
				region = world_middle_east_arabia
				region = world_europe_north
				region = world_europe_south
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_artifact = VIET_wolf_pelt }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
			
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.3
			viet_artifact_loss_three_flags = yes
		}				
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.3
			any_artifact = {
				has_artifact_flag = VIET_clutter_flag
			}
		}			
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = hunter
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			capital_scope = {
				OR = {
					region = world_europe_north
					region = world_steppe
				}
			}
		}	
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			is_strong_trigger = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			is_weak_trigger = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = craven
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = cruel
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
	}
	
	option = { #ok
		name = VIETmisc.8116.a
		add_artifact = VIET_wolf_pelt		
	}	
	option = { #don't need it
		name = VIETmisc.8116.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = proud
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = proud
				chance = 45
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			80 = { }
			10 = { add_trait = content }
			10 = { add_trait = humble }
		}		
	}
}

		}

			factor = 1.2
			trait = ambitious

			trait = content
		}

			factor = 1.2

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = envious
		}

			factor = 0.8
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2

		}
		modifier = {

			trait = shy
		}
	}

		}

			70 = { }
			10 = { add_trait = just }
			10 = { add_trait = humble }
			10 = { add_trait = content }
		}		
	}
}

	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1

			factor = 0.3
			viet_artifact_loss_three_flags = yes
		}

			trait = gregarious
		}

			trait = shy
		}

		}
		modifier = {

			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2

		}

		}

		}

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {

			trait = cruel
		}
	}
	
	option = { #ok

# Find an ostracon outside
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8128
	desc = VIETmisc.8128.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_tuscan_country
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no
		
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		NOT = { has_artifact = VIET_ostracon }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
			
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.3
			viet_artifact_loss_three_flags = yes
		}				
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.3
			any_artifact = {
				has_artifact_flag = VIET_clutter_flag
			}
		}				
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.3
			location = {
				NOR = {
					region = world_africa_west
					region = world_steppe_east
					region = world_steppe_west
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = humble
		}
	}
	
	option = { #keep it
		name = VIETmisc.8128.a
		add_artifact = VIET_ostracon
		new_artifact = {
			set_creation_date = 1.1.1
		}		
	}	
	option = { #give it to scholars
		name = VIETmisc.8128.b
		prestige = 5
		random = {
			culture_techpoints = 100
			chance = 50
		}
	}	
	option = { #destroy it
		name = VIETmisc.8128.c
		piety = 5
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = cynical
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = cynical
				chance = 70
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = zealous }
			}
			random = {
				add_trait = zealous
				chance = 25
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = paranoid }
			}
			random = {
				add_trait = paranoid
				chance = 45
			}
		}
	}
}


# Farmer uses Nok terracotta statue as a scarecrow - loosely based on how the Nok culture was discovered in the first place
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8129
	desc = VIETmisc.8129.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_dogon_village
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no
		
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		NOT = { has_artifact = VIET_nok_terracotta_figure }
		capital_scope = {
			region = world_africa_west
		}
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
			
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.3
			viet_artifact_loss_three_flags = yes
		}				
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.3
			any_artifact = {
				has_artifact_flag = VIET_clutter_flag
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			higher_real_tier_than = DUKE
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_tribal = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = paranoid
		}
	}
	
	option = { #looks nice
		name = VIETmisc.8129.a
		random_list = {
			10 = { add_trait = trusting }
			10 = { add_trait = content }
			10 = { add_trait = humble }
			70 = { }
		}		
	}	
	option = { #buy it from the farmer
		name = VIETmisc.8129.b
		wealth = -3
		add_artifact = VIET_nok_terracotta_figure
		new_artifact = {
			set_creation_date = 1.1.1
		}
	}	
	option = { #force farmer to give it
		name = VIETmisc.8129.c
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				trait = kind
				trait = just
				trait = charitable
			}
		}
		piety = -4
		random_list = {
			25 = { add_trait = cruel }
			25 = { add_trait = greedy }
			25 = { add_trait = arbitrary }
			25 = { }
		}
		add_artifact = VIET_nok_terracotta_figure
		new_artifact = {
			set_creation_date = 1.1.1
		}
	}
	option = { #persuade farmer
		name = VIETmisc.8129.d
		tooltip_info = diplomacy
		trigger = {
			diplomacy = 10
		}
		add_artifact = VIET_nok_terracotta_figure
		new_artifact = {
			set_creation_date = 1.1.1
		}
	}
}
