# Meet someone you know irl in a dream
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8220
	desc = VIETmisc.8220.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_small_town
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # What a coincidence! Good reaction
		name = VIETmisc.8220.a
		FROM = {
			random = {
				add_friend = ROOT
				chance = 30
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_shared_dream_good
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
			reverse_opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_shared_dream_good
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # What a coincidence! Bad reaction
		name = VIETmisc.8220.b
		FROM = {
			random = {
				add_rival = ROOT
				chance = 15
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_shared_dream_bad
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
			reverse_opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_shared_dream_bad
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
		}
	}
}


# Dream of a Korean Drama (probably should've been considered an event chain but oh well)
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8221
	desc = VIETmisc.8221.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_modern_slice_of_life
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
	
	trigger = {
		#in_command = no
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
		#Might be immersion breaking for some 
		NOT = {
			has_game_rule = {
				name = VIET_events_rules
				value = serious
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_generic_kdrama_happened_to_me }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1	
				
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = cruel
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = lustful
		}
	}

	option = { # Who am I?
		name = VIETmisc.8221.a
		set_character_flag = VIET_generic_kdrama_happened_to_me
		custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_kdrama_who_am_i }
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.3
						is_female = yes
						NOT = { trait = homosexual }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.3
						is_female = no
						trait = homosexual
					}
					#set_character_flag = VIET_kdrama_girls_pov
					character_event = { id = VIETmisc.8222 } # girl's POV
				}
				50 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.3
						is_female = no
						NOT = { trait = homosexual }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.3
						is_female = yes
						trait = homosexual
					}
					#set_character_flag = VIET_kdrama_boys_pov
					character_event = { id = VIETmisc.8225 } # boy's POV
				}
			}		
		}
	}
}

# What is reality and what is dream?
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8231
	desc = VIETmisc.8231.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_recovery
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Reality
		name = VIETmisc.8231.a
		random = {
			add_trait = proud
			chance = 5
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_campfire_dream
			duration = 777
		}
	}
	option = { # Dream
		name = VIETmisc.8231.b
		random = {
			add_trait = lunatic
			chance = 5
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_campfire_dream
			duration = 777
		}
	}
	option = { # Cannot distinguish between the two
		name = VIETmisc.8231.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				learning = 11
				trait = erudite
				trait = scholar
				trait = theologian
				trait = lunatic
				religion = tao #Zhuangzi
				religion = tao_reformed
			}
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_navel_gazing
			duration = 777
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_campfire_dream
			duration = 777
		}
	}
	option = { # Dream within a dream
		name = VIETmisc.8231.d
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				learning = 11
				trait = erudite
				trait = scholar
				trait = theologian
				trait = lunatic
				religion = tao #Zhuangzi
				religion = tao_reformed
			}
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_navel_gazing
			duration = 777
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_campfire_dream
			duration = 777
		}
	}
}

			factor = 1.2
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = gluttonous
		}
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.8233.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = wroth
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = wroth
				chance = 25
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = content
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = content
				chance = 25
			}
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_primordial_river_dream
			duration = 852
		}
	}
}

# Chinese shoemakers want to build a small shrine to Liu Bei
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8240
	desc = VIETmisc.8240.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_small_town_chinese_group
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no	
		NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_liu_bei_shoemakers }		
		capital_scope = {
			OR = {
				region = custom_eastern_edge_of_map
				region = world_steppe_tarim
				is_sinosphere_large_trigger = yes
			}
		}	
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }	
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1	
				
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = envious
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = VIET_liu_bei_shoemakers
	}

	option = { # Don't help
		name = VIETmisc.8240.a		
	}
	option = { # Provide a bit of aid
		name = VIETmisc.8240.b
		wealth = -10
		prestige = 20
		capital_scope = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = VIET_liu_bei_shoemaker_shrine_small
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Provide lots of aid
		name = VIETmisc.8240.c
		wealth = -25
		prestige = 50
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = arbitrary
			}
			remove_trait = arbitrary
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				add_trait = just
				chance = 40
			}
		}
		capital_scope = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = VIET_liu_bei_shoemaker_shrine_large
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
	}
}


# Chinese travelers offer a statue of Guan Yu
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8241
	desc = VIETmisc.8241.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_travel_chinese_group
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no	
		NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_guan_yu_statue_event }		
		capital_scope = {
			OR = {
				region = custom_eastern_edge_of_map
				region = world_steppe_tarim
				region = world_steppe_east
				region = world_persia
				region = world_india
				#is_sinosphere_large_trigger = yes
			}
		}	
		NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }	
		NOT = { has_artifact = VIET_guan_yu_statue }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
			
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.3
			viet_artifact_loss_three_flags = yes
		}				
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.3
			any_artifact = {
				has_artifact_flag = VIET_clutter_flag
			}
		}				
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			location = {
				NOR = {
					region = custom_eastern_edge_of_map
					region = world_steppe_tarim
				}
			}
		}
				
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = greedy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = envious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = craven
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = VIET_guan_yu_statue_event
	}

	option = { # Heathen statue!
		name = VIETmisc.8241.a	
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				religion_group = indian_group
				religion = bon
				religion = bon_reformed
				religion_group = zoroastrian_group
				trait = sympathy_indian
				trait = cynical
			}
		}
		piety = 10
		prestige = -10
		random = {
			add_trait = zealous
			chance = 40
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = patient
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = patient
				chance = 50
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = humble
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = humble
				chance = 50
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Thank but reject
		name = VIETmisc.8241.b	
		piety = 5
	}
	option = { # Accept
		name = VIETmisc.8241.c	
		add_artifact = VIET_guan_yu_statue
		new_artifact = {
			set_creation_date = 1.1.1
		}	
	}
}


# Chinese poet recites poetry inspired by the Three Caos
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8242
	desc = VIETmisc.8242.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_asian_calligraphy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no			
		capital_scope = {
			OR = {
				region = custom_eastern_edge_of_map
				region = world_steppe_tarim
				is_sinosphere_large_trigger = yes
			}
		}	
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }	
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1				
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = poet
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = scholar
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = hunter
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = erudite
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = stubborn
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = chaste
		}
	}

	option = { # Don't like poetry
		name = VIETmisc.8242.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_dislikes_hipsters
			duration = 365
		}
	}
	option = { # Like poetry
		name = VIETmisc.8242.b
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_appreciates_fine_art
			duration = 365
		}
	}
	option = { # Recruit poet
		name = VIETmisc.8242.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_cao_cao_poetry_option }
			NOT = {
				any_courtier = {
					has_character_flag = VIET_cao_cao_poet
				}
			}
		}
		wealth = -20	
		prestige = -20
		create_character = {
			dynasty = random
			religion = ROOT
			culture = han
			female = no
			health = 5
			random_traits = no
			historical = yes
			attributes = {
				diplomacy = 7
				learning = 8
			}
		}
		new_character = {
			#Education & other basic stuff
			set_character_flag = VIET_cao_cao_poet
			set_character_flag = no_court_invites
			random_list = {
				25 = { add_trait = charismatic_negotiator }
				25 = { add_trait = grey_eminence }
				25 = { add_trait = scholarly_theologian }
				25 = { add_trait = mastermind_theologian }
			}	
			#Guaranteed Traits
			add_trait = poet
			#Clutter Artifact					
			random = {
				VIET_give_clutter_artifact_effect = yes
				chance = 10
			}
			#Randomize appearance
			random_list = {
				20 = { set_graphical_culture = bodpa }
				50 = { }
			}
			#Flavor
			random_list = {
				800 = { } #Nothing
				100 = { add_scarred_tiered_effect = yes }
				20 = { 
					trigger = { has_dlc = Reapers }
					add_trait = one_eyed
				}
				20 = { 
					trigger = { has_dlc = Reapers }
					add_trait = one_handed
				}
				20 = { 
					trigger = { has_dlc = Reapers }
					add_trait = one_legged
				}
				5 = { 
					trigger = { has_dlc = Reapers }
					add_trait = one_legged
					add_trait = one_handed
				}
				5 = { 
					trigger = { has_dlc = Reapers }
					add_trait = one_legged
					add_trait = one_eyed
				}
				5 = { 
					trigger = { has_dlc = Reapers }
					add_trait = one_eyed
					add_trait = one_handed
				}
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_loyal_servant
				who = ROOT
				years = 100
			}			
			if = {
				limit = { has_dlc = "Way of Life" }
				random_list = {
					50 = { add_trait = scholar }
					25 = { add_trait = socializer }
					10 = { add_trait = administrator }
					10 = { add_trait = hunter }
					10 = { add_trait = duelist }
					10 = { add_trait = gardener }
					300 = {}
				}
			}
			#Personality Archetypes
			random_list = {
				20 = { # Noble and virtuous
					set_character_flag = VIET_cao_cao_poet_nobleman
					add_trait = humble
					add_trait = kind
					add_trait = chaste
					add_trait = just
					add_trait = charitable
				}
				20 = { # Cunning and realistic
					set_character_flag = VIET_cao_cao_poet_pragmatist
					add_trait = cynical
					add_trait = patient
					add_trait = erudite
					add_trait = deceitful
					add_trait = paranoid
				}
				20 = { # Brave and ambitious
					set_character_flag = VIET_cao_cao_poet_risktaker
					add_trait = ambitious
					add_trait = brave
					add_trait = proud
					add_trait = stubborn
					add_trait = diligent
				}
				20 = { # Taoist hermit
					set_character_flag = VIET_cao_cao_poet_hermit
					religion = tao
					add_trait = celibate
					add_trait = mystic
					add_trait = patient
					add_trait = temperate
					add_trait = content
					add_trait = honest
					add_trait = brave
				}
				20 = { # Cultured and roguish
					set_character_flag = VIET_cao_cao_poet_suave
					add_trait = erudite
					add_trait = lustful
					add_trait = slothful
					add_trait = patient
					add_trait = gregarious
				}
				20 = { # Drunken fool
					set_character_flag = VIET_cao_cao_poet_li_bai
					add_trait = drunkard
					add_trait = erudite
					add_trait = lustful
					add_trait = slothful
					add_trait = patient
					add_trait = gregarious
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

			}

		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }

		}

			opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_doesnt_value_relationship
				who = ROOT
				years = 3
			}

			OR = {
				region = custom_eastern_edge_of_map

				is_sinosphere_large_trigger = yes
			}
		}	
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }	
		NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_three_kingdoms_inspiration }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1

				is_sinosphere_small_trigger = yes			
			}

		}

			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}

		}

			factor = 0.8

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = poet
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8

		}
		modifier = {

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8

	immediate = {

		}
	}

		}
	}

	option = { # Women

		}
	}
}

# Will Constantinople ever be taken by a Muslim lord?
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8249
	desc = VIETmisc.8249.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_hagia_sofia
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
	religion_group = muslim
	
	trigger = {
		#in_command = no
		NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
		NOT = {
			496 = {
				OR = {
					owner = {
						religion_group = muslim
					}
					owner = {
						any_liege = {
							religion_group = muslim
						}
					}				
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1				
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			capital_scope = {
				NOR = {
					region = world_asia_minor
					region = world_europe_south
					region = world_steppe_west
					region = world_middle_east
					region = world_persia
					region = world_africa_north
				}
			}
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = erudite
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = stubborn
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = paranoid
		}
	}

	option = { # Perhaps one day
		name = VIETmisc.8249.a
	}
	option = { # Constantinople is too mighty
		name = VIETmisc.8249.b
		prestige = -2
		random_list = {
			10 = { add_trait = craven }
			10 = { add_trait = slothful }
			10 = { add_trait = cynical }
			10 = { add_trait = patient }
			60 = { }
		}
	}
	option = { # More important things to worry about
		name = VIETmisc.8249.c
		piety = -2
		random_list = {
			15 = { add_trait = just }
			15 = { add_trait = diligent }
			15 = { add_trait = cynical }
			55 = { }
		}
	}
	option = { # I could conquer it!
		name = VIETmisc.8249.d
		random_list = {
			10 = { add_trait = brave }
			20 = { add_trait = proud }
			70 = { }
		}
	}
}


# Dispute between Italian merchants and Byzantine administrators
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8250
	desc = VIETmisc.8250.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_busy_trading_dock_republic
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
		OR = {
			top_liege = {
				has_landed_title = e_byzantium
			}
			AND = {
				culture_group = byzantine
				capital_scope = {
					OR = {
						region = world_asia_minor
						region = world_europe_south_east
					}
				}			
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1				
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			NOT = {
				has_landed_title = c_byzantion
			}
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = erudite
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = stubborn
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = paranoid
		}
	}

	option = { # Support Italians
		name = VIETmisc.8250.a
		prestige = -10
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_italian_merchant_support
			duration = 730
		}
	}
	option = { # Support Byzantine nobles
		name = VIETmisc.8250.b
		prestige = -10
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_byzantine_noble_support
			duration = 730
		}
	}
	option = { # Neither
		name = VIETmisc.8250.c
		prestige = -5
		random_list = {
			15 = { add_trait = slothful }
			15 = { add_trait = trusting }
			15 = { add_trait = craven }
			55 = { }
		}
	}
	option = { # Invite Italian merchant to act as representative
		name = VIETmisc.8250.d
		trigger = {
			diplomacy = 11
			NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_italian_merchant_representative_option }
		}
		tooltip_info = diplomacy
		custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_italian_merchant_negotiation_cool }
		set_character_flag = VIET_italian_merchant_representative_option
		prestige = 10
		capital_scope = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = VIET_negotiated_italian_deals
				duration = 1825
			}
		}
		create_random_steward = {
			dynasty = actually_culture
			religion = catholic
			culture = italian
			female = no
			random_traits = yes
			historical = yes
		}
		new_character = {
			#Education & other basic stuff
			set_character_flag = ai_flag_refuse_concubinage
			set_character_flag = ai_flag_refuse_marriage
			set_character_flag = no_court_invites
			#Guaranteed Traits
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_loyal_servant
				who = ROOT
				years = 100
			}
			#Clutter Artifact					
			random = {
				VIET_give_clutter_artifact_effect = yes
				chance = 10
			}
			#Flavor
			random_list = {
				90 = { add_scarred_tiered_effect = yes }
				10 = { 
					trigger = { has_dlc = Reapers }
					add_trait = one_eyed
				}
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_italian_merchant_negotiator
				duration = -1
			}
			#Randomize appearance
			random_list = {
				5 = { set_graphical_culture = german }
				5 = { set_graphical_culture = frankish }
				5 = { set_graphical_culture = levantine_arabic }
				5 = { set_graphical_culture = greek }
				5 = { set_graphical_culture = serbian }
				5 = { set_graphical_culture = polish }
				55 = { }
			}	
		}
	}
}

			top_liege = {
				OR = {
					has_landed_title = e_byzantium
					has_landed_title = e_roman_empire

			chance = 20
		}
	}

		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_thinking_about_foreign_lands
			duration = 365
		}

			chance = 20

	capable_only = yes

	#war = no

		#in_command = no
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
	#}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1				
	
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = erudite
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = paranoid
		}
	}

	option = { # Barbaric
		name = VIETmisc.8252.a
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				religion_group = zoroastrian_group
				has_religion_feature = religion_holy_family 
			}	
		}
		piety = 3
	}
	option = { # Open minded
		name = VIETmisc.8252.b
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				religion_group = zoroastrian_group
				has_religion_feature = religion_holy_family
			}	
		}
		piety = -3
		prestige = -3
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_religiously_tolerant_ruler
			duration = 365
		}
	}
	option = { # Horny
		name = VIETmisc.8252.c
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					religion_group = zoroastrian_group
					has_religion_feature = religion_holy_family 
				}
			}
			piety = -5
			prestige = -5
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_deviant_opinion
				duration = 365
			}
			random = {
				add_trait = lustful
				chance = 30
			}
		}
		else = {
			piety = 3
			prestige = 3
			random = {
				add_trait = lustful
				chance = 20
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Skeptical
		name = VIETmisc.8252.d
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_skeptical_ruler
			duration = 365
		}
		random = {
			add_trait = cynical
			chance = 20
		}
	}
	option = { # Faithful followers
		name = VIETmisc.8252.e
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				religion_group = zoroastrian_group
				has_religion_feature = religion_holy_family

			factor = 1.2
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = envious
		}
	}

	option = { # Type A is bad
		name = VIETmisc.8259.a
		piety = 5
		random_list = {
			50 = { }
			25 = { add_trait = patient }
			25 = { add_trait = humble }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = ambitious
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = ambitious
				chance = 50
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Type A is good
		name = VIETmisc.8259.b
		piety = 5
		random_list = {
			50 = { }
			25 = { add_trait = brave }
			25 = { add_trait = arbitrary }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = patient
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = patient
				chance = 40
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = temperate
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = temperate
				chance = 40
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = humble
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = humble
				chance = 40
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # You met the Dreamer?
		name = VIETmisc.8259.c
		trigger = { # Dreamer - will have to change later, will not trigger atm
			has_character_flag = VIET_met_the_dreamer
		}
	}
}

	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1				
	
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = humble
		}
	}

	option = { # Rewrite
		name = VIETmisc.8266.a
		prestige = -5
		wealth = -5
		random = {
			add_trait = stressed
			chance = 20
		}
	}
	option = { # Leave as is
		name = VIETmisc.8266.b
		prestige = -10
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = ambitious
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = ambitious
				chance = 40
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				add_trait = content
				chance = 40
			}
		}
	}
}

# Testing an upright official incognito
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8269
	desc = VIETmisc.8269.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_gathering_of_minds
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1				
	
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = wroth
		}
	}

	option = { # It's an act
		name = VIETmisc.8269.a
		trigger = {
			trait = proud
		}
		tooltip_info = proud
		random = {
			add_trait = cynical
			chance = 30
		}
	}
	option = { # Good!
		name = VIETmisc.8269.b
		prestige = 5
	}
	option = { # Reward him
		name = VIETmisc.8269.c
		prestige = 5
		wealth = -10
		random = {
			add_trait = charitable
			chance = 30
		}
	}
	option = { # Invite him to court
		name = VIETmisc.8269.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_invited_upright_official_to_court }
		}
		set_character_flag = VIET_invited_upright_official_to_court
		prestige = -25
		create_random_steward = {
			dynasty = actually_culture
			religion = ROOT
			culture = ROOT
			female = no
			random_traits = no
			historical = yes
			attributes = {
				diplomacy = 8
				martial = 4
				stewardship = 9
				intrigue = 6
				learning = 7
			}
		}
		new_character = {
			#Education & other basic stuff
			set_character_flag = ai_flag_refuse_concubinage
			set_character_flag = ai_flag_refuse_marriage
			#set_character_flag = no_court_invites
			#Guaranteed Traits
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_loyal_servant
				who = ROOT
				years = 100
			}
			#Clutter Artifact					
			random = {
				VIET_give_clutter_artifact_effect = yes
				chance = 10
			}
			add_trait = just
			add_trait = humble
			add_trait = honest
			add_trait = patient
			add_trait = kind
			add_trait = administrator
			#Flavor
			random_list = {
				100 = { }
				23 = { add_scarred_tiered_effect = yes }
				2 = { 
					trigger = { has_dlc = Reapers }
					add_trait = one_eyed
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				5 = { add_trait = genius }
				10 = { add_trait = quick }
				25 = { add_trait = shrewd }
				60 = {}
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_upright_official
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

# Minor official overlooked because of humble origin
character_event = {

	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes

	war = no

		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1				
	
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = arbitrary
		}
	}

	option = { # Lineage is most important
		name = VIETmisc.8275.a
		prestige = 5
		piety = -5
		random = {
			add_trait = proud
			chance = 30
		}
	}
	option = { # Promote the minor official
		name = VIETmisc.8275.b
		prestige = -5
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_promoted_minor_official
			duration = 1000
		}
	}
	option = { # Let them sort it out
		name = VIETmisc.8275.c
	}
	option = { # Invite to court
		name = VIETmisc.8275.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_invited_talented_humble_official }
		}
		set_character_flag = VIET_invited_talented_humble_official
		prestige = -20
		wealth = -5
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_promoted_minor_official
			duration = 1000
		}
		create_character = {
			dynasty = actually_culture
			religion = ROOT
			culture = ROOT
			female = no
			random_traits = yes
			historical = yes
		}
		new_character = {
			#Education & other basic stuff
			set_character_flag = ai_flag_refuse_concubinage
			set_character_flag = ai_flag_refuse_marriage
			#set_character_flag = no_court_invites
			#Guaranteed Traits
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_loyal_servant
				who = ROOT
				years = 100
			}
			#Clutter Artifact					
			random = {
				VIET_give_clutter_artifact_effect = yes
				chance = 10
			}
			#Flavor
			random_list = {
				100 = { }
				23 = { add_scarred_tiered_effect = yes }
				2 = { 
					trigger = { has_dlc = Reapers }
					add_trait = one_eyed
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				50 = { add_trait = genius }
				50 = { add_trait = quick }
			}
			random = {
				add_trait = strong
				chance = 30
			}
			random = {
				add_trait = fair
				chance = 30
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_talented_humble_official
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

		days = 1				
	
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}

			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = envious
		}
	}

	option = { # buy some
		name = VIETmisc.8278.a

			40 = { health = 0.15 }
			30 = { health = 0.3 }

			10 = { health = 0.6 }
		}
	}

	option = { # just looking
		name = VIETmisc.8278.b
	}
	
	option = { # quack medicine
		name = VIETmisc.8278.c

				trait = trusting
			}

				remove_trait = trusting
				chance = 30
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			70 = { }
			15 = { add_trait = cynical }
			15 = { add_trait = proud }
		}
	}
}

# Blacksmiths renowned in province
province_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8282
	desc = VIETmisc.8282.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_weaponsmith
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = VIET_province_blacksmiths_renowned }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 8000
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			OR = {
				terrain = steppe
				terrain = arctic
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			NOT = { num_of_max_settlements = 3 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			owner = {
				OR = {
					is_nomadic = yes
					is_tribal = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Cool
		name = VIETmisc.8282.a
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = VIET_province_blacksmiths_renowned
			duration = 5475
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Reapers"
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = increase_prosperity_custom_tooltip
				hidden_tooltip = {
					change_variable = { which = prosperity_value value = 8 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Is China the greatest?
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8285
	desc = VIETmisc.8285.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_china_stable
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			culture_group = chinese
		}
		#in_command = no
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1				
	
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				religion_group = muslim #historically the Muslims thought China was super cool, which is why they didn't mind the Khitan so much
				culture_group = altaic
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			capital_scope = {
				OR = {
					region = world_africa_west
					region = world_africa_north
					region = world_europe_east
					region = world_europe_north
					region = world_europe_west
				}
			}
		}	
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = erudite
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = stubborn
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = paranoid
		}
	}

	option = { # We should be proud of ourselves
		name = VIETmisc.8285.a
		prestige = 5
		random = {
			add_trait = proud
			chance = 20
		}
	}
	option = { # We have much to learn from them
		name = VIETmisc.8285.b
		piety = 5
		random = {
			add_trait = humble
			chance = 20
		}
	}
	option = { # No better than anyone else
		name = VIETmisc.8285.c
		random = {
			add_trait = cynical
			chance = 40
		}
	}
}

	}

		}

		}

		}

		}
	}

		name = VIETmisc.8286.a

		}

				chance = 25
			}
		}
	}

		name = VIETmisc.8286.b
		prestige = 10

			}
			remove_trait = wroth
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				add_trait = just
				chance = 25
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Physician did his best, give him credit
		name = VIETmisc.8286.c
		prestige = 10
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = wroth
			}
			remove_trait = wroth
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				add_trait = trusting
				chance = 25
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Ackshually...
		name = VIETmisc.8286.d
		trigger = {
			trait = physician
		}
		tooltip_info = physician
		prestige = 20
	}
	option = { # Ackshually...
		name = VIETmisc.8286.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = { trait = physician }

	}

		trigger = {
			learning = 12
			NOT = { trait = physician }
			NOT = { trait = scholar }
		}

		prestige = 20
	}
}

# Maid reports your courtier wrote her a creepy love letter
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8290
	desc = VIETmisc.8290.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_gift
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no
	
	trigger = {
		any_courtier = {
			is_adult = yes
			useless_character_trigger = no
			NOT = { trait = celibate }
			NOT = { trait = chaste }
			NOT = { trait = kind }
			OR = {
				trait = shy
				trait = lustful
				trait = hedonist
				trait = proud
				trait = stubborn
			}
			has_lover = no
			OR = {
				is_female = no
				AND = {
					is_female = yes
					trait = homosexual
				}
			}
		}
		#in_command = no
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1				
	
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = envious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = paranoid
		}
	}

	option = { # her problem
		name = VIETmisc.8290.a
		piety = -5
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = just
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = just
				chance = 50
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # talk to courtier
		name = VIETmisc.8290.b
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_adult = yes
				useless_character_trigger = no
				NOT = { trait = celibate }
				NOT = { trait = chaste }
				NOT = { trait = kind }
				OR = {
					trait = shy
					trait = lustful
					trait = hedonist
					trait = proud
					trait = stubborn
				}
				has_lover = no
				OR = {
					is_female = no
					AND = {
						is_female = yes
						trait = homosexual
					}
				}
			}
			prestige = -5
			piety = -5
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_loves_cute_maids
				duration = 365
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_angry
				who = ROOT
				years = 3
			}	
			reverse_opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_angry
				who = ROOT
				years = 3
			}		
		}
	}
}

# Tavern owner gives present of wooden bowl

	id = VIETmisc.8297

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no
		
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		NOT = { has_artifact = VIET_wooden_bowl }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
			
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.3
			viet_artifact_loss_three_flags = yes
		}				
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.3
			any_artifact = {
				has_artifact_flag = VIET_clutter_flag
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
	}
	
	option = { #ok
		name = VIETmisc.8297.a
		prestige = -10
		random = {
			add_trait = humble
			chance = 15
		}
		add_artifact = VIET_wooden_bowl		
	}
	
	option = { #ok
		name = VIETmisc.8297.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = humble
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = humble
				chance = 50
			}	
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				add_trait = proud
				chance = 50
			}	
		}
	}	
}

		}

			trait = cynical
		}

			}
		}
	}

# Ancient Desert Statue - guard finds it while lost
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8302
	desc = VIETmisc.8302.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_sand_desert
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
		
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		NOT = { has_artifact = VIET_ancient_statue_desert }
		capital_scope = {
			OR = {
				terrain = desert
				region = world_middle_east
				region = world_persia
				region = world_africa
				region = world_india_north
				region = world_steppe_tarim
			}
			NOT = { terrain = mountain }
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
			
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.3
			viet_artifact_loss_three_flags = yes
		}				
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.3
			any_artifact = {
				has_artifact_flag = VIET_clutter_flag
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			capital_scope = {
				OR = {
					region = world_africa_north
					region = world_middle_east
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			NOT = { learning = 7 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = erudite
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = stubborn
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = cruel
		}
	}
	
	option = { #ok
		name = VIETmisc.8302.a
		add_artifact = VIET_ancient_statue_desert	
		new_artifact = {
			set_creation_date = 1.1.1
		}			
	}
	
	option = { #ok
		name = VIETmisc.8302.b
		random = {
			add_trait = charitable
			chance = 25
		}
	}	
}


# Ancient European (Celtic) stone head - peasant finds a mustached statue
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8303
	desc = VIETmisc.8303.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_prospering_province
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
		
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		NOT = { has_artifact = VIET_celtic_stone_head }
		capital_scope = {
			OR = {
				region = world_europe
				region = world_asia_minor
				region = world_steppe_west
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
			
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.3
			viet_artifact_loss_three_flags = yes
		}				
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.3
			any_artifact = {
				has_artifact_flag = VIET_clutter_flag
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			capital_scope = {
				region = world_europe_west
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			NOR = {
				is_tribal = yes
				is_nomadic = yes
				capital_scope = {
					OR = {
						region = world_europe_west_brittania
						region = world_europe_west_francia
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = erudite
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = stubborn
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = cruel
		}
	}
	
	option = { #keep it
		name = VIETmisc.8303.a
		add_artifact = VIET_celtic_stone_head
		new_artifact = {
			set_creation_date = 1.1.1
		}				
	}	
	
	option = { #keep it but compensate peasant
		name = VIETmisc.8303.b
		wealth = -10
		piety = 5
		add_artifact = VIET_celtic_stone_head
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = greedy
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = greedy
				chance = 40
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = charitable }
			}
			random = {
				add_trait = charitable
				chance = 25
			}
			random = {
				add_trait = humble
				chance = 15
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				add_trait = humble
				chance = 30
			}		
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Let peasant lady keep it
		name = VIETmisc.8303.c
		random_list = {
			65 = { }
			10 = { add_trait = humble }
			10 = { add_trait = kind }
			15 = { add_trait = charitable }
		}
	}	
	
	option = { #Throw it away!
		name = VIETmisc.8303.d
		piety = 5
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = cynical
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = cynical
				chance = 40
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = zealous }
			}
			random = {
				add_trait = zealous
				chance = 25
			}
			random = {
				add_trait = paranoid
				chance = 15
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				add_trait = paranoid
				chance = 30
			}		
		}
	}	
}

# Nobleman runs away from criminals trying to kill him
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8313
	desc = VIETmisc.8313.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_hiding_from_pursuers
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1				
	
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = craven
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = cruel
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = kind
		}
	}

	option = { # send guards
		name = VIETmisc.8313.a
		wealth = -10
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_leader_who_cares
			duration = 1000
		}
	}
	option = { # ignore
		name = VIETmisc.8313.b
		prestige = -30
		random = {
			add_trait = arbitrary
			chance = 40
		}
	}
	option = { # invite nobleman
		name = VIETmisc.8313.c
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_leader_who_cares
			duration = 1000
		}
		create_character = {
			age = 22
			dynasty = actually_culture
			religion = ROOT
			culture = ROOT
			random_traits = yes
			historical = yes
		}
		new_character = {
			#Education & other basic stuff
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_nobleman_with_criminal_problems
				duration = -1
			}
			set_character_flag = ai_flag_refuse_concubinage
			set_character_flag = ai_flag_refuse_marriage
			set_character_flag = VIET_lydia_character
			set_character_flag = no_court_invites
			random = {
				VIET_give_clutter_artifact_effect = yes
				chance = 10
			}		
			#Guaranteed Traits
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_loyal_servant
				who = ROOT
				years = 100
			}
		}
	}
}

			is_nomadic = no

		}
	}

		months = 12000

			factor = 1.2
			NOT = { num_of_max_settlements = 5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			NOT = { num_of_max_settlements = 3 }
		}
	}

		}

# Friend falls asleep on shoulder
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8318
	desc = VIETmisc.8318.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_apollo_sun
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Let them sleep
		name = VIETmisc.8318.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Zeus"
			}
			random_list = {
				10 = { add_trait = conscientious }
				10 = { add_trait = affectionate }
				10 = { add_trait = indolent }
				10 = { add_trait = timid }
				20 = { }
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_list = {
				10 = { add_trait = kind }
				10 = { add_trait = patient }
				10 = { add_trait = shy }
				10 = { add_trait = slothful }
				20 = { }
			}	
		}
	}
	option = { # Gently wake them up
		name = VIETmisc.8318.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Zeus"
			}
			random_list = {
				10 = { add_trait = conscientious }
				10 = { add_trait = affectionate }
				10 = { add_trait = brooding }
				10 = { add_trait = fussy }
				20 = { }
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_list = {
				10 = { add_trait = kind }
				10 = { add_trait = patient }
				10 = { add_trait = humble }
				10 = { add_trait = trusting }
				20 = { }
			}	
		}
	}
	option = { # Prank them
		name = VIETmisc.8318.c
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Zeus"
			}
			random_list = {
				10 = { add_trait = curious }
				10 = { add_trait = haughty }
				10 = { add_trait = playful }
				10 = { add_trait = affectionate }
				20 = { }
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_list = {
				10 = { add_trait = arbitrary }
				10 = { add_trait = gregarious }
				10 = { add_trait = proud }
				10 = { add_trait = deceitful }
				20 = { }
			}	
		}
	}
}


# Courtier plays in rain puddles
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8319
	desc = VIETmisc.8319.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_garden
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no		
		capital_scope = {
			NOT = { terrain = desert }
			NOT = { terrain = arctic }
		}
		any_courtier = {
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			is_adult = yes
			in_command = no
			is_abroad = no
			NOR = {
				trait = diligent
				trait = depressed
				trait = cynical
				trait = paranoid
				trait = shy
			}
		}
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1				
	
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = craven
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = proud
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				is_adult = yes
				in_command = no
				is_abroad = no
				NOR = {
					trait = diligent
					trait = depressed
					trait = cynical
					trait = paranoid
					trait = shy
				}
			}
			save_event_target_as = target_VIET_rain_puddle_dancer
		}	
	}

	option = { # Immature!
		name = VIETmisc.8319.a
		event_target:target_VIET_rain_puddle_dancer = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_publically_chastised_me
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
			reverse_opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_disappointed
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Whatever
		name = VIETmisc.8319.b
	}

	option = { # Join in!
		name = VIETmisc.8319.c
		prestige = -5
		event_target:target_VIET_rain_puddle_dancer = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_likes_to_be_silly_with_me
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
			reverse_opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_likes_to_be_silly_with_me
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = shy
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = shy
				chance = 33
			}
		}
	}
}

# Ancient cistern found
province_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8321
	desc = VIETmisc.8321.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_skyrim_forest
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = VIET_province_ancient_cistern_restored }
		NOR = {
			region = world_steppe_east
			region = world_steppe_west
			region = world_europe_north
			region = world_europe_east
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 8000
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			NOT = { num_of_max_settlements = 5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			NOT = { num_of_max_settlements = 3 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				region = world_europe_west_brittania
				region = world_europe_west_germania
			}
		}
	}
	

	option = { # Lend financial support
		name = VIETmisc.8321.a
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				wealth = 30
			}
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = VIET_province_ancient_cistern_restored
			duration = 3650
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Reapers"
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = increase_prosperity_custom_tooltip
				hidden_tooltip = {					
					change_variable = { which = prosperity_value value = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		owner = {
			wealth = -30
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_leader_who_cares
				duration = 730
			}
			random = {
				add_trait = charitable
				chance = 20
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Lend lots of financial support
		name = VIETmisc.8321.b
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				wealth = 60
			}
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = VIET_province_ancient_cistern_restored
			duration = 7300
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Reapers"
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = increase_prosperity_custom_tooltip
				hidden_tooltip = {					
					change_variable = { which = prosperity_value value = 4 }
				}
			}
		}
		owner = {
			wealth = -60
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_leader_who_cares
				duration = 1460
			}
			random = {
				add_trait = charitable
				chance = 40
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Don't do anything
		name = VIETmisc.8321.c
	}
}

			terrain = arctic
		}

		}

		}

		}

	}			
	option = { # Reverse engineer recipe

		trigger = {
			trait = genius
		}

	}

		trigger = {

		}

# Mazoga the orc knight joins your court
long_character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8345
	desc = VIETmisc.8345.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_castle_construction
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { # thank her but send her off
		name = VIETmisc.8345.a
		prestige = 10
		wealth = -10
	}
	option = { # thank her and accept her in your court
		name = VIETmisc.8345.b
		prestige = -20
		create_random_soldier = {
			#age = 30
			dynasty = actually_culture
			religion = ROOT
			culture = random
			female = yes
			random_traits = no
			historical = yes
			attributes = {
				diplomacy = 2
				martial = 7
			}
		}
		new_character = {
			#Education & other basic stuff
			set_character_flag = ai_flag_refuse_concubinage
			set_character_flag = ai_flag_refuse_marriage
			set_character_flag = no_court_invites
			set_character_flag = special_marshal
			#Guaranteed Traits
			add_trait = strong
			add_trait = brave
			add_trait = wroth
			add_trait = just
			add_trait = stubborn
			add_trait = diligent
			add_trait = adventurer
			add_artifact = bow_tier_2_new
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_loyal_servant
				who = ROOT
				years = 100
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_mazoga_the_orc
				duration = -1
			}
			#Flavor
			random_list = {
				50 = { }
				45 = { add_scarred_tiered_effect = yes }
				5 = { 
					trigger = { has_dlc = Reapers }
					add_trait = one_eyed
				}
			}
			#random = {
			#	add_trait = ugly
			#	chance = 25
			#}
		}
	}
}

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no

		in_command = no
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }

			name = VIET_events_rules
			value = silly
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {

		}

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = paranoid
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ignore her

		prestige = 5
	}

		piety = 5
	}

		name = VIETmisc.8348.c

			age = 28
			dynasty = actually_culture
			religion = ROOT
			culture = ROOT
			female = yes
			random_traits = no
			historical = yes
		}

			#Education & other basic stuff

				10 = { add_random_education_trait = intrigue }

			}
			add_trait = lunatic
			add_trait = gregarious
			add_trait = kind
			add_trait = humble
			add_trait = trusting
			give_nickname = VIET_runs_in_circles_nickname
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_loyal_servant
				who = ROOT
				years = 100
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_runs_in_circles
				duration = -1
			}
			add_artifact = VIET_calipers
			#random = {
			#	VIET_give_clutter_artifact_effect = yes
			#	chance = 10
			#}	
			#Flavor
			random_list = {
				70 = { }
				25 = { add_scarred_tiered_effect = yes }
				5 = { 
					trigger = { has_dlc = Reapers }
					add_trait = one_eyed
				}

				trait = greedy
			}
			random = {

				chance = 50
			}
		}
	}
}

			}

			random = {
				add_trait = paranoid
				chance = 30
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Relax

		piety = 1
		random_list = {
			60 = { }
			20 = { add_trait = content }
			10 = { add_trait = humble }

# Find a beggar's corpse on the side of the road
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8367
	desc = VIETmisc.8367.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_dead_body_hf
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1				
	
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = trusting
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.8367.a
		prestige = 4
	}
	
	option = { # dispose of it!
		name = VIETmisc.8367.b
		prestige = 2
		piety = 2
	}
	
	option = { # bury it properly
		name = VIETmisc.8367.c
		trigger = {
			wealth = 5
		}
		wealth = -5
		piety = 10
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = cruel
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = cruel
				chance = 50
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = proud
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = proud
				chance = 50
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			60 = { }
			10 = { add_trait = humble }
			10 = { add_trait = kind }
			10 = { add_trait = charitable }
			10 = { add_trait = just }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = muslim
			}
			decadence = -1
		}
		custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_beggars_deserve_dignified_burials_too }
	}
}

# Ghosts keep visiting a province
province_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8370
	desc = VIETmisc.8370.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_village_at_night
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = VIET_province_ghostly_visitors_blessing }
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = VIET_province_ghostly_visitors_curse }
		#NOR = {
		#	region = world_steppe_east
		#	region = world_steppe_west
		#	region = world_europe_north
		#	region = world_europe_east
		#	region = world_himalayas
		#}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 10000
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			NOT = { num_of_max_settlements = 5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			NOT = { num_of_max_settlements = 3 }
		}
	}
	

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.8370.a
		random_list = {
			10 = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = VIET_province_ghostly_visitors_blessing
					duration = 1825
				}			
			}
			10 = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = VIET_province_ghostly_visitors_curse
					duration = 1825
				}			
			}
		}
	}
}

		in_command = no
		NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
		religion_group = baltic_group
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1				
	
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = honest
		}
	}
	
	option = { # leave
		name = VIETmisc.8373.a
	}	
	option = { # do it
		name = VIETmisc.8373.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					is_female = no
					NOT = { trait = homosexual }
				}
				AND = {
					is_female = yes
					trait = homosexual
				}
			}
			NOR = {
				trait = chaste
				trait = celibate
				trait = eunuch
			}
		}
		add_trait = lustful
		prestige = 5
		hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = VIETmisc.8374 } }
	}
}

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes

		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }

			culture = saxon
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {

# Coming across a Myling (Nordic mythology)
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8376
	#desc = VIETmisc.8376.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_artemis_moon
	
	# Religious based
	desc = {
		text = VIETmisc.8376.desc.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				religion = norse_pagan
				religion = norse_pagan_reformed		
			}		
		}
	}
	#Cultural based if not pagan
	desc = {
		text = VIETmisc.8376.desc.b
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				religion = norse_pagan
				religion = norse_pagan_reformed		
			}		
		}
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
		OR = {
			culture_group = north_germanic
			culture_group = finno_ugric
			religion = norse_pagan
			religion = norse_pagan_reformed
		}
		any_courtier = {
			is_adult = yes
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			ai = yes
			OR = {
				religion = ROOT
				culture = ROOT
			}
			OR = {
				trait = zealous
				trait = brave
				trait = kind
				trait = lunatic
				trait = possessed
				trait = charitable
			}
			NOT = { trait = cynical }
			NOT = { trait = craven }
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1				
	
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = wroth
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_adult = yes
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				ai = yes
				OR = {
					religion = ROOT
					culture = ROOT
				}
				OR = {
					trait = zealous
					trait = brave
					trait = kind
					trait = lunatic
					trait = possessed
					trait = charitable
				}
				NOT = { trait = cynical }
				NOT = { trait = craven }
			}
			save_event_target_as = target_VIET_myling_courtier
		}
	}
	
	option = { # haha funny
		name = VIETmisc.8376.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = highly_amused_ruler
			duration = 365
		}
		event_target:target_VIET_myling_courtier = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_didnt_believe_me
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # it's a lie
		name = VIETmisc.8376.b
		prestige = 5
		event_target:target_VIET_myling_courtier = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_didnt_believe_me
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # just a strange dream
		name = VIETmisc.8376.c
		piety = 5
		event_target:target_VIET_myling_courtier = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_believes_me
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }

	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1				
	
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = craven
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = arbitrary
		}
	}
	
	option = { # waste of time
		name = VIETmisc.8377.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { trait = humble }
			NOT = { trait = kind }
			NOT = { trait = charitable }
		}
		random = {
			add_trait = proud
			chance = 40
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = muslim
			}
			decadence = 1
		}
	}
	
	option = { # carry on
		name = VIETmisc.8377.b
		prestige = 4
	}
	
	option = { # can I join in?
		name = VIETmisc.8377.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { trait = zealous }
		}
		piety = 4
		random_list = {
			80 = { }
			10 = { add_trait = zealous }
			10 = { add_trait = humble }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = muslim
			}
			decadence = -1
		}
	}
}

	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes

		#in_command = no
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }

		NOT = { trait = immortal }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1				
	
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = proud
		}

			factor = 0.8
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = slothful
		}

			}

		}

			}

		}

		}
	}

			factor = 1.2
			NOT = { num_of_max_settlements = 5 }
		}
		modifier = {

			NOT = { num_of_max_settlements = 3 }
		}
	}
	

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.8392.a
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = VIET_province_death_of_several_officials
			duration = 1825
		}

			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Reapers"
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = decrease_prosperity_custom_tooltip
				hidden_tooltip = {
					change_variable = { which = prosperity_value value = -4 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

		name = VIETmisc.8392.b
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				trait = administrator
			}
		}
		tooltip_info = administrator
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = VIET_province_death_of_several_officials
			duration = 1095
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Reapers"
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = decrease_prosperity_custom_tooltip
				hidden_tooltip = {
					change_variable = { which = prosperity_value value = -2 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.8392.b
		trigger = {

				NOT = { trait = administrator }
			}
		}

		}

			}

# Come across a black cat
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8397
	desc = VIETmisc.8397.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_cat
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
	
	trigger = {
		#in_command = no
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
		# Cultures where black cats are seen as good, or cats are revered in general
		NOR = {
			culture_group = celtic
			culture_group = west_germanic
			culture = norman
			culture_group = arabic
			culture_group = ethiopic
			culture_group = chinese
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1				
	
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = cruel
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = just
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.8397.a
		random_list = {
			10 = { piety = -2 }
			10 = { prestige = -2 }
		}
	}
	
	option = { # no fear!
		name = VIETmisc.8397.b
		random_list = {
			75 = { }
			20 = { add_trait = brave }
			5 = { add_trait = trusting }
		}
		custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_silly_rationality_about_black_cat }
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				40 = { }
				30 = { health = 0.3 }
				20 = { health = 0.6 }
				10 = { health = 1 }
				30 = { health = -0.3 }
				20 = { health = -0.6 }
				10 = { health = -1 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Servant's pet dog passed away
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8402
	desc = VIETmisc.8402.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_hunting_scene
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1				
	
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = stubborn
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = erudite
		}
	}
	
	option = { # stupid dog
		name = VIETmisc.8402.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = kind
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = kind
				chance = 40
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				add_trait = cruel
				chance = 30
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # shape up or i'll punish you
		name = VIETmisc.8402.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { trait = kind }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = patient
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = patient
				chance = 40
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				add_trait = wroth
				chance = 30
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # find you a new dog
		name = VIETmisc.8402.c
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = wroth
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = wroth
				chance = 40
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				add_trait = patient
				chance = 30
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # take your time
		name = VIETmisc.8402.d
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = cruel
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = cruel
				chance = 30
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			70 = { }
			20 = { add_trait = kind }
			10 = { add_trait = patient }
		}
	}

character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8408
	desc = VIETmisc.8408.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_doctor_crazy_treatment
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
		is_nomadic = no
		is_tribal = no
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1				
	
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			learning = 12
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			NOT = { learning = 7 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = paranoid
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.8408.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = craven
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = craven
				chance = 25
			}
		}
		random = {
			add_trait = gregarious
			chance = 40
		}
		random = {
			change_learning = 1
			chance = 20
		}
	}	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.8408.b
		random_list = {
			60 = { }
			10 = { add_trait = craven }
			10 = { add_trait = proud }
			10 = { add_trait = paranoid }
			10 = { add_trait = diligent }
		}
	}
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.8408.c
		trigger = {
			learning = 11
			NOT = { trait = physician }
			NOT = { trait = scholar }
		}
		tooltip_info = learning
		prestige = 5
		random = {
			change_learning = 1
			chance = 50
		}		
	}
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.8408.c
		trigger = {
			trait = scholar
			NOT = { trait = physician }
		}
		tooltip_info = scholar
		prestige = 5
		random = {
			change_learning = 1
			chance = 50
		}		
	}
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.8408.c
		trigger = {
			trait = physician
		}
		tooltip_info = physician
		prestige = 5
		random = {
			change_learning = 1
			chance = 50
		}		
	}
}

# Courtier takes wrong type and dosage of medicine by accident
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8410
	desc = VIETmisc.8410.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
		any_courtier = {
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			is_adult = yes
			in_command = no
			is_abroad = no
			ai = yes
			OR = {
				is_dumb_trigger = yes
				has_mental_disorder_trigger = yes
				trait = slothful
				trait = trusting
				trait = wroth
				trait = stubborn
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1				
	
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = envious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = gregarious
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.8410.a
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				is_adult = yes
				in_command = no
				is_abroad = no
				ai = yes
				OR = {
					is_dumb_trigger = yes
					has_mental_disorder_trigger = yes
					trait = slothful
					trait = trusting
					trait = wroth
					trait = stubborn
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				60 = { }
				20 = { health = -0.1 }
				10 = { health = -0.3 }
				10 = { health = -0.5 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Panch Poron - traditional east Indian and Nepali spice mix
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8414
	desc = VIETmisc.8414.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_herbs_and_spices
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
	
	trigger = {
		#in_command = no
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
		OR = {
			culture_group = indoaryan
			culture_group = dravidian
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1				
	
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			# Mainly used in eastern India and Nepal
			NOT = {
				culture = bengali
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = wroth
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.8414.a
		random = {
			add_trait = content
			chance = 10
		}
	}
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.8414.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = content
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = content
				chance = 25
			}
		}
		random = {
			add_trait = wroth
			chance = 10
		}
	}
}

# Quick thinking servant saves another servant by using caraway seeds
long_character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8416
	desc = VIETmisc.8416.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
		NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_servant_caraway_savior }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1				
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = cruel
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = VIET_servant_caraway_savior
	}
	
	option = { # who cares
		name = VIETmisc.8416.a
		piety = -5
		random = {
			add_trait = proud
			chance = 20
		}
	}	
	option = { # reward him
		name = VIETmisc.8416.b
		prestige = -5
		wealth = -10
		piety = 5
		random = {
			add_trait = charitable
			chance = 40
		}
	}	
	option = { # make him a courtier
		name = VIETmisc.8416.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				ai = no
				wealth = 10
			}
			OR = {
				trait = charitable
				trait = kind
				trait = humble
				trait = trusting
				trait = arbitrary
			}
			NOR = {
				trait = proud
				trait = cruel
				trait = envious
			}
		}
		wealth = -10
		prestige = -20
		random_list = {
			10 = { #Young female servant
				create_character = {
					age = 20
					dynasty = none
					religion = ROOT
					culture = ROOT
					female = yes
					health = 5.5
					random_traits = no
					historical = yes
				}
				new_character = {
					#Education & other basic stuff
					add_character_modifier = {
						name = VIET_quick_witted_savior
						duration = -1
					}
					set_character_flag = ai_flag_refuse_concubinage
					set_character_flag = ai_flag_refuse_marriage
					set_character_flag = VIET_quick_witted_savior_character
					set_character_flag = no_court_invites
					random_list = {
						10 = { add_random_education_trait = intrigue }
						10 = { add_random_education_trait = stewardship }
						10 = { add_random_education_trait = learning }
					}					
					random = {
						VIET_give_clutter_artifact_effect = yes
						chance = 10
					}		
					#Guaranteed Traits
					random_list = {
						10 = { add_trait = genius }
						40 = { add_trait = quick }
						50 = { add_trait = shrewd }
					}
					add_trait = diligent
					add_trait = brave
					add_trait = kind
					add_trait = patient
					random_list = {
						10 = { add_trait = fair }
						20 = { add_trait = groomed }
						70 = { }
					}
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_loyal_servant
						who = ROOT
						years = 100
					}
				}
