# Gifted shampoo made from kaffir lime
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8417
	desc = VIETmisc.8417.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_throne_room
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
	
	trigger = {
		#in_command = no
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1				
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = chaste
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Nice
		name = VIETmisc.8417.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_kaffir_lime_shampoo
			duration = 525
		}
	}	
	option = { # Give to spouse
		name = VIETmisc.8417.b
		trigger = {
			any_spouse = {
				is_adult = yes
				ai = yes
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
			}		
		}
		random_spouse = {
			limit = {
				is_adult = yes
				ai = yes
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_kaffir_lime_shampoo_gift
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_kaffir_lime_shampoo
				duration = 525
			}
		}
	}	
	option = { # Give to courtier
		name = VIETmisc.8417.c
		trigger = {
			any_courtier = {
				is_adult = yes
				ai = yes
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
			}		
		}
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_adult = yes
				ai = yes
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_kaffir_lime_shampoo_gift
				who = ROOT
				years = 3
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_kaffir_lime_shampoo
				duration = 525
			}
		}
	}
}


# Lovage plant used to season dishes in the Balkans
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8418
	desc = VIETmisc.8418.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_VIET_food
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
	
	trigger = {
		#in_command = no
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
		OR = {
			culture_group = byzantine
			culture_group = south_slavic
			capital_scope = {
				OR = {
					culture_group = byzantine
					culture_group = south_slavic
				}			
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1				
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = cruel
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Nice
		name = VIETmisc.8418.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = eating_good_food
			duration = 222
		}
	}	
	option = { # Peasant food!
		name = VIETmisc.8418.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = humble
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = humble
				chance = 75
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				add_trait = proud
				chance = 40
			}
		}
	}
}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = gluttonous
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Nice
		name = VIETmisc.8420.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_majoram_tea
			duration = 365
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = stressed
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = stressed
				chance = 30
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = depressed
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = depressed
				chance = 30
			}
		}
	}
}

	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1				
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = envious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = kind
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Nice
		name = VIETmisc.8422.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				ai = no
				wealth = 10
			}
		}
		wealth = -10
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_musk_mallow
			duration = 1825
		}
	}	
	option = { # Buy for spouse
		name = VIETmisc.8422.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				ai = no
				wealth = 10
			}
			is_married = yes
			any_spouse = {
				ai = yes
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
			}
		}
		wealth = -10
		random_spouse = {
			limit = {
				ai = yes
				NOT = { trait = incapable }			
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_musk_mallow_gift
				who = ROOT
				years = 3
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_musk_mallow
				duration = 1825
			}		
		}
	}
	option = { # Not interested
		name = VIETmisc.8422.c
		piety = 5
		random_list = {
			80 = { }
			10 = { add_trait = humble }
			10 = { add_trait = content }
		}
	}
}

# Eating too much nutmeg causes adverse effects
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8425
	desc = VIETmisc.8425.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_VIET_food
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
		NOT = { trait = temperate }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1	
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = greedy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = charitable
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = diligent
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.8425.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ill = no
				NOT = {
					has_dlc = "Reapers"
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				75 = { }
				25 = { add_trait = ill }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ill = no
				has_dlc = "Reapers"
			}
			
			random_list = {
				75 = { }
				25 = { 
					set_character_flag = disease_not_serious
					add_trait = vomiting
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = RIP.11005 days = 5 random = 5 } }
		}		
	}
}

# Courtier picks up board games as a hobby
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8437
	desc = VIETmisc.8437.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_war_planning
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
		any_courtier = {
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			NOT = { trait = gamer }
			is_adult = yes
			in_command = no
			is_abroad = no
			NOT = { is_close_relative = ROOT }
			ai = yes
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1	
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = honest
		}
	}
	
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				NOT = { trait = gamer }
				is_adult = yes
				in_command = no
				is_abroad = no
				NOT = { is_close_relative = ROOT }
				ai = yes
			}
			save_event_target_as = target_VIET_new_gamer_courtier
		}
	}
	
	option = { # cool
		name = VIETmisc.8437.a
		prestige = 2
		event_target:target_VIET_new_gamer_courtier = {
			add_trait = gamer
			opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_played_game
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
			reverse_opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_played_game
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}		
		}
	}	
	option = { # not cool
		name = VIETmisc.8437.b
		piety = 2
		event_target:target_VIET_new_gamer_courtier = {
			add_trait = gamer
			opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_doesnt_approve_games
				who = ROOT
				years = 3
			}
			reverse_opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_gamer_loser
				who = ROOT
				years = 3
			}		
		}
	}
	option = { # teach some tricks
		name = VIETmisc.8437.c
		trigger = {
			trait = gamer
		}
		tooltip_info = gamer
		prestige = 4
		event_target:target_VIET_new_gamer_courtier = {
			add_trait = gamer
			opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_taught_me_game_tricks
				who = ROOT
				years = 2
			}
			#reverse_opinion = {
			#	modifier = VIET_opinion_learning_game_tricks
			#	who = ROOT
			#	years = 2
			#}		
		}
	}
}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = craven
		}
	}
	
	
	option = { # tell them to stop
		name = VIETmisc.8440.a
		random = {
			add_trait = wroth
			chance = 25
		}
	}

		name = VIETmisc.8440.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { trait = chaste }
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = lustful_ruler
			duration = 365
		}
		random = {
			add_trait = lustful
			chance = 25
		}
	}	
	option = { # forget it
		name = VIETmisc.8440.c
		random = {
			add_trait = content
			chance = 25
		}
	}
	option = { # give them blessing
		name = VIETmisc.8440.d
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = cruel
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = cruel
				chance = 40
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				add_trait = kind
				chance = 40
			}
		}
	}
}

			factor = 1.2

		}

			factor = 0.8
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2

		}
		modifier = {

		}

		}

# Traveler helps guards take down gang of female thieves who use seduction (Oblivion/Anvil reference)
long_character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8445
	desc = VIETmisc.8445.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_maiden
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_anvil_sirens_event }
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1	
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = slothful
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = VIET_anvil_sirens_event
	}
		
	option = { # no reward
		name = VIETmisc.8445.a
		prestige = -15
		piety = -10
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = charitable
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = charitable
				chance = 66
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				add_trait = greedy
				chance = 33
			}
		}
	}	
	option = { # standard gold reward
		name = VIETmisc.8445.b
		wealth = -15
	}	
	option = { # ask them to provide guards some tips
		name = VIETmisc.8445.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				ai = no
				wealth = 30
			}
		}
		wealth = -30
		prestige = -10
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_personal_guards_get_adventurer_tips
			duration = 4745
		}
	}	
	option = { # hire them
		name = VIETmisc.8445.d
		custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_siren_anvil_adventurer_hire }
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				# Female version
				50 = {
					create_random_intriguer = {
						age = 28
						dynasty = actually_culture
						religion = ROOT
						culture = ROOT
						female = yes
						random_traits = yes
						historical = yes
						attributes = {
							diplomacy = 6
							intrigue = 7
						}
					}
					new_character = {
						#Education & other basic stuff
						set_character_flag = ai_flag_refuse_concubinage
						set_character_flag = ai_flag_refuse_marriage
						set_character_flag = no_court_invites
						set_character_flag = special_spymaster #special_marshal
						#Guaranteed Traits
						add_trait = adventurer				
						random = {
							VIET_give_generic_weapon_effect = yes
							chance = 20
						}						
						opinion = {
							modifier = opinion_loyal_servant
							who = ROOT
							years = 100
						}
						add_character_modifier = {
							name = VIET_anvil_siren_helper_female
							duration = -1
						}
						#Flavor
						random_list = {
							60 = { }
							30 = { add_scarred_tiered_effect = yes }
							10 = { 
								trigger = { has_dlc = Reapers }
								add_trait = one_eyed
							}
						}
					}			
				}
				# Male version
				50 = {
					create_random_soldier = {
						age = 28
						dynasty = actually_culture
						religion = ROOT
						culture = ROOT
						female = no
						random_traits = yes
						historical = yes
						attributes = {
							martial = 7
							intrigue = 6
						}
					}
					new_character = {
						#Education & other basic stuff
						set_character_flag = ai_flag_refuse_concubinage
						set_character_flag = ai_flag_refuse_marriage
						set_character_flag = no_court_invites
						#Guaranteed Traits
						add_trait = adventurer				
						random = {
							VIET_give_generic_weapon_effect = yes
							chance = 20
						}						
						opinion = {
							modifier = opinion_loyal_servant
							who = ROOT
							years = 100
						}
						add_character_modifier = {
							name = VIET_anvil_siren_helper_male
							duration = -1
						}
						#Flavor
						random_list = {
							60 = { }
							30 = { add_scarred_tiered_effect = yes }
							10 = { 
								trigger = { has_dlc = Reapers }
								add_trait = one_eyed
							}
						}
					}			
				}			
			}
		}
	}
}

# Province becomes well-known for its baklava
province_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8450
	desc = VIETmisc.8450.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_baklava
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = VIET_province_famous_baklava }
		owner = {
			is_nomadic = no
		}
		is_baklava_culture_trigger = yes
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 12000
	}
	

	option = { # Spend funds to help
		name = VIETmisc.8450.a
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = VIET_province_famous_baklava
			duration = 3650
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Reapers"
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = increase_prosperity_custom_tooltip
				hidden_tooltip = {					
					change_variable = { which = prosperity_value value = 4 }
				}
			}
		}
	}	
}

# 
# Farewell/Swansong Letter
# 
# For anyone reading this, first of all, I wish to say thank you for all your support -
# whether you recently discovered my mods, or have been with me from the very beginning
# when I created my first CK2 mod in August of 2012, back when I was still in college.
# It's been a long journey of on and off modding of CK2, and modding this game was one
# part of some of the most interesting and life-changing periods of my life, both good
# and bad. As someone who enjoys creative writing, modding CK2 was one of my many outlets
# to express myself as a writer during this time. While I'll miss CK2 modding, I intend to
# continue modding in CK3 - who knows what life will be like years from now, if I still mod CK3?
# With that, once more, thanks for all the support over the years, and wish all the best.
# 
# - Cybrxkhan
# 
######################################################################################################################
